Important Foreign Telegrams 2

Report of the British Imperial Conference 79

Preferential Treatment Continued for Three Years, No Results from Economic Events Discussions

▲ Reuters, London, 14th: The report of the Imperial Conference states that overseas representatives have made the same agreement because Britain has undertaken to continue the existing preferential treatment for three years, but it must be subject to the sanctions of the parliament's own budget-making power, and within three years, it must not reduce the preferential treatment given to Britain, in order to show its response to the committee's report in favor of British flour mills, part of the wheat used must be produced in the Empire, and undertake to give it careful consideration. As for constitutional issues, the Governor-General will be appointed by the Emperor in accordance with the advice of the relevant autonomous territory's cabinet members, and the communication channel between the Emperor and the autonomous territory will be purely a matter between the Emperor and the government of the autonomous territory. The Imperial Conference approved the imperial broadcasting of radio services. Regarding this matter, the conference has asked the British Broadcasting Corporation whether the Imperial Broadcasting Corporation is willing to fund this expense. The Imperial Conference acknowledged the current economic difficulties and did not allow British immigrants to flock to the autonomous territories, but is confident that immigrants will be accommodated in the future. The Imperial Conference proposed to pass the petition drafted by the Legislative Committee of the Autonomous Territories last year, one of which advocated that any changes to the law on the succession to the throne or the title of the Emperor must be approved by the Parliament of the Autonomous Territories. The Imperial Conference also approved the establishment of an Imperial Court to resolve any disputes between the autonomous territories within the Empire, but the dispute must be automatically submitted to the court by the parties concerned.

▲ Reuters, London, 14th: At the last plenary session of the Imperial Conference, the Prime Ministers of the autonomous territories all gave speeches, stating that although there were no results in the economic aspect, there was no need to be disappointed, because they knew that the governments must adopt the principle of giving priority to their own people, and they knew before the meeting that the British government held special views on tax rates, because it had to consider the interests of the British people. Australian Prime Minister Scullin and Canadian Prime Minister Bennett both advocated the allocation of wheat import quotas as a substitute for tax rates. Indian representative Shafique said that India hoped to obtain the full status of overseas autonomous territory soon, and said that the whole of India, including the princes and the people, was paying attention to the day when it could send representatives to participate in the Imperial Conference like other autonomous territories. The Imperial Conference has a lot of work to do, and it seems that it should be held frequently, instead of waiting for four years.

Important Domestic News

The New French Envoy Presents His Credentials 80

The newly appointed French Minister to China, Mr. Wilder, accompanied by Counselor Mr. Lippitschaye, Secretary Mr. Ducquier, Military Attaché Mr. Kexue, etc., went to Nanjing from Shanghai. On the 15th, they went to the National Government to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and present their credentials. The details are as follows:

▲ The Ceremony of Audience: The National Government first prepared several large cars and sent Section Chief Liu Naifan of the Bureau of Ceremonies to the French Minister's residence at 9:00 a.m. to welcome them. Infantry and military bands were stationed on both sides of the driveway inside the gate of the National Government. When the French Minister arrived at the residence, they played music to pay tribute. The National Government sent Adjutant Tang Zhi and Section Chief Liu Naifan to be in charge of the reception. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent Secretary Jin Zhi and Social Section Chief Bi Mingyu as interpreters. After the French Minister got out of the car, he went to the reception room to rest. The Director of the Bureau of Ceremonies went in to inform him. Soon, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, wearing military uniform, came to the hall. All the civil and military officials of the National Government, all in ceremonial dress, were arranged in the east and west. The Minister of Foreign Affairs and the foreign affairs translators stood on the right side of the Chairman. After the arrangement was completed, the Director of the Bureau of Ceremonies went in to inform the French Minister to have an audience. The French Minister entered the hall door, bowed to the Chairman, bowed again in the hall, and bowed three times in front of the Chairman. The Chairman returned the salute one by one. The Minister of Foreign Affairs read out the title of the French Minister. After the reading, the French Minister gave a congratulatory speech and then presented his credentials. After the Chairman received the credentials, he handed them over to the Minister of Foreign Affairs. Then the Chairman delivered a reply speech in Chinese, which was translated by the translator. The Chairman then shook hands with the French Minister and talked with him. Liu Naifan conveyed the message. The Chairman asked about the health of the President of France and exchanged pleasantries for a moment. The French Minister said goodbye, shook hands and bowed back, then bowed again in the hall, and bowed three times at the hall door. The Chairman returned the salute one by one. After the ceremony, the Director of the Bureau of Ceremonies and the reception officer led the French Minister back to the reception room. The Minister of Foreign Affairs and the officials of the National Government, the Army Commander, etc., also entered the reception room to socialize. The French Minister then said goodbye and was escorted back to his residence by the reception staff.

▲ The French Minister's Congratulatory Speech: Your Excellency Chairman, the President of my country has appointed me to reside in your country as Minister Plenipotentiary. Now, I present the credentials I have brought and the letter of resignation from the former Minister. I would like to mention that this is my first time in China. Thirty-one years ago, most of my life's footsteps were in China, and I have traveled all over the interior. Therefore, I am deeply familiar with and admire the working spirit of your country's people. Since 1911, I have been fortunate to hear the speeches and demeanor of your Excellency, who has been able to devote all his efforts to completing this great cause of building a new China, and who has recently announced the success of this great cause. Your Excellency and all the colleagues who work with you are loyal successors of Premier Sun, who founded the Republic of China and whose name will be immortalized. With the help of all of you, the national fortune of your country will surely open a prosperous and great new era in terms of work and progress. During my tenure, my responsibility is to maintain and further consolidate the inherent friendship between China and France. I know that the government and people of my country all expect this from me. I must be more diligent and hope that your Excellency will give me assistance so that I can complete the sincere cooperation between the two countries and consolidate the peace of the world. Now, I respectfully represent the President of my country and wish your country a prosperous national fortune and your Excellency a healthy body.

▲ The Chairman's Reply: Your Excellency Minister, the President of your country has appointed you as Minister Plenipotentiary of the Republic of China and personally presented the letter of appointment and the letter of resignation of the former Minister. I am very pleased to receive them. Your Excellency has been in China for many years, has extensive contacts, and is familiar with the wishes of our country and its people. In the future, you will be able to perform your duties faithfully. As Your Excellency hopes, the government of your country is very fortunate to have selected the right person. I firmly believe that Your Excellency's residence in China will surely make the inherent friendship between China and France more consolidated. Furthermore, I would like to tell Your Excellency that our government will be able to provide all the conveniences that Your Excellency needs in your official duties within the possible scope. Now, with sincere sincerity, I wish your country a prosperous national fortune, the President of your country a healthy body, and Your Excellency a peaceful journey.

The Anti-Opium Association Asks to Stop the Opium Tax in Northern Anhui 81

The Central Anti-Opium Commission has received reports from local groups in Hefei, Bo County, and other places that the troops stationed in northern Anhui are levying opium taxes from various counties. The committee has submitted a request to the Executive Yuan for instructions. Now, representatives from Yicheng and other counties have successively telegraphed to report the previous situation. The committee has submitted the matter to the 60th committee meeting for discussion and decided to submit it to the General Headquarters and the Executive Yuan, and to the Anhui Provincial Government, ordering them to strictly stop the levy. Yesterday, the committee has submitted the decision to the General Headquarters and the Executive Yuan, ordering them to strictly stop the levy, and to the Anhui Provincial Government for handling.

Jiangxi People Living in Beijing Petition for the Suppression of Bandits 82

Yesterday at 6:00 p.m., the Jiangxi Compatriots Association in Beijing and the Jiangxi Disaster Relief Association held a banquet at Changsong East, Confucius Temple, to entertain Liu Zhi, a member of the Central Committee, Liu Zuozhou, a member of the Provincial Committee, and representatives from the Wuhan, Shanghai, Yangzhou, and Hunan representative groups, totaling more than 50 people. The representatives reported on the tragic situation of various places being ravaged by the Communist bandits, with tears in their eyes. The atmosphere in the whole room was gloomy. Then, Liu Zhi explained that the Central Government did not look down on the bandit situation in Jiangxi Province. The representatives were satisfied. After the banquet, a joint meeting was held. Each group elected one chairman to form a presidium, which included Fu Dingsheng (Beijing), Hu Jiesan (Wuhan), Zeng Yuchen (Shanghai), Ma Anbang (Yangzhou), and Li Yue (Hunan). They also divided into three sections: general affairs, publicity, and documents, and set up a joint office. It was decided to host important Jiangxi figures and newspaper reporters in Beijing at the Central Hotel at noon on the 16th. Next Monday, they will jointly launch a large-scale petition. The petition to the National Government from the Yangzhou representative is recorded below:

"We believe that the disaster of the Communist bandits in Jiangxi has been going on for a long time, and its poison is greater than ever. Ji'an, the center of the Gan River, has been lost, and Qingjiang, the intersection of the Yuan River, has been heard to have fallen many times. Famous cities have fallen one after another, and the provincial capital has been shaken. Where will our elders flee to their death? Looking around the West River, how much clean land is left? We, the people of the association, are staying outside, and we can steal our lives for a while, but where can we go home? In the past, when the state of Chu fell, Bao Xu still cried for the Qin army. Now, we are all under the same banner, how can Zhang and Gong be abandoned? Therefore, we, with our remnant bodies, make a heartfelt appeal. On the 9th of this month, we held a general meeting of Jiangxi compatriots in Yangzhou at the Jiangxi Guild Hall, and unanimously decided to list ten items and publicly elect representatives to rush to your government and present them to you one by one. (1) Please quickly send a large army to recover the lost land as soon as possible. Ji'an is the center of culture, transportation, industry, and commerce on the Gan River. After bandit alarms were discovered in western and southern Jiangxi, refugees from various counties and townships gathered in the county town, and the population became more numerous and the wealth increased. Since it was captured by the Communist bandits on October 4, the high-rise buildings were burned to the ground, and outstanding members were brutally killed. Merchants with some property were tied up as hostages, and farmers and workers who were ignorant were incorporated into the Red Army. They were still imprisoned women and raped at will, and condoned peasant bandits to kill at will. For more than a month, we have heard of hundreds of people being killed and hundreds of households being looted every day. The suffering and duration of the disaster have reached such an extent. Whose fault is this? Although it is not necessary to say, the authorities quickly send a large army one day, they can save the lives of the people for one more day. Recovering one inch of lost land one day earlier can save one place from ruins. This is the first thing that we are eager to petition for. (2) Please send a special commissioner to the front line to take charge of the command. Ji'an is located in the middle reaches of the Gan River, and it is the hub of Hunan, Hubei, Fujian, and Guangdong. Now it has been occupied by the Communist bandits as their base camp. To the east, they can enter Fujian, to the west, they can go out to Hunan, to the south, they can invade Guangdong, and to the north, they can plan the Yangtze River. It is not only a major disaster for Jiangxi, but also a deep concern for those who plan the country. If it is not regarded as the same as the overall situation, and the provinces were allowed to make their own plans in the past, it has caused the bandits to grow stronger, and trampled on Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi to such an extreme. If it continues to spread, what a terrible disaster it will be? The people pay taxes to support the army, and the state trains the army to defend the people. It is excusable if the military strength is insufficient, but the National Revolutionary Army has won hundreds of battles and destroyed hundreds of thousands of enemy troops with one blow, let alone tens of thousands of bandits. This is all because there is no special commander, and those who hold concurrent posts do not regard the importance of the overall situation, which has led to this situation. Can you specially appoint Liu Zhi, a victorious general from Jiangxi, to the front line to take charge of the command? This is the second thing that we are eagerly waiting to petition for. (3) Please thoroughly eliminate the Communist bandits within a time limit and do not leave any future troubles.

The Communist bandits had no real strength at first, but they lurked in the mountains and took advantage of opportunities to think. If the local military police had known to cut off their roots early, how could a spark have started a prairie fire? And after they became a large force, it was clear that they were like wild boars and long snakes, and they were only clowns jumping around, or they concealed their illness, or they flaunted their merits, or they only cherished their strength, or they used neighboring provinces as ditches. They nurtured the tumor and became a problem to this day. Now, to learn from the past and be careful in the future, we should not divide provincial boundaries and eliminate them within a time limit. And the elimination must be thorough, and there must be no guns left, and no bandits disturbing, so that we can say that we have exhausted the responsibility of suppressing bandits. Otherwise, the previous lessons can be learned, and future troubles are worthy of worry. This is the third thing that we are eager to petition for. (4) Please issue strict orders to reward those who have made contributions and punish those who are cowardly. The troops stationed have the responsibility to defend the territory, and the people rely on them to entrust their lives. They are free to advance and retreat, placing the people in water and fire, which is a crime that cannot be escaped. Even if they are ordered to suppress bandits, the armies are the cadres of the country and have the sacred duty to defend the people. Compared to those who oppose the rebellion, there is no difference. If, as before, they abandon the city and lose the land, without condemning anyone, how can we calm the anger of the refugees and achieve the success of the suppression? Now, we should issue strict orders, reward merits and punish crimes, and carry them out vigorously, so that we can be successful. This is the fourth thing that we are eager to petition for. (5) Please raise enough military expenses and avoid increasing the local burden. Jiangxi Province has been disturbed by bandits for several years, agriculture has been abandoned in the fields, commerce has been suspended in the markets, production has been cut off, and the storage has been empty for a long time. In terms of essence, it can be said that it has been lost. Now, in addition to tens of thousands of Communist bandits, the places they pass through are ruins. Even if there are remnants, they only have skin and bones. At this time, when the army is passing through, the supply of food will inevitably be difficult. Please raise enough military expenses, so as not to delay the military opportunity, and to avoid increasing the local burden. This is the fifth thing that we are eager to petition for. (6) Please strictly prohibit the army from burning houses in the disaster area. Before the 15th year of the Republic of China, Jiangxi Province had a family that was well-fed and clothed, and we had never heard of bandits. Later, because the Communist bandits invaded the people and advocated the theory of robbing property and inciting robbery and murder, the officials did not ask, and the military police did not save. Therefore, it became more and more intense. The wise people abandoned their homes and avoided places to avoid disaster, and the kind and cowardly people joined the gang to steal their lives. They are called bandit dens, but they are actually disaster areas. In the past, when the bandit suppression troops saw houses that had been stationed by bandits, they were all set on fire. The Communist bandits already knew this point and deliberately set up false opportunities in the homes of the people who were escaping outside, in order to use the burning by the National Army as a propaganda mouth. The local people know this evil plan the most, so they dare to sincerely present it. Even if it is indeed a Communist bandit house, why can't it be confiscated according to law to show punishment? At this time, when material resources are difficult and construction is not easy, we hope that strict orders will be issued to not burn people's houses. This is the sixth thing that we are eager to petition for. (7) Please strengthen the people's self-defense forces and strictly implement the Qingxiang. The people of Jiangxi are accustomed to a peaceful life and lack self-defense ability. Therefore, once they are robbed by the Communist bandits, it is easy to coerce them and difficult to extricate themselves. Now, the plan is to rely on the government to strengthen its self-defense forces in one place, and send personnel to clear the countryside, guide legal organizations, and distribute the guns and weapons seized from the Communist bandits to the people's militia. Because at this time of desolation, there is no financial resources to buy guns, and the Communist bandits' guns were mostly seized from the people's militia, so we dare to make this request, so as to make up for the inadequacy of the army. This is the seventh thing that we are eager to petition for. (8) Please strictly assess the responsibility of the Jiangxi Provincial authorities and quickly seek good aftercare. The state sets up officials and divides responsibilities, each with its own special duties. Defending the territory and protecting the people is their unshirkable responsibility. The bandit disaster in Jiangxi Province did not come suddenly or unexpectedly. Why did Ji'an, the center of the Gan River, abandon the city in a panic once it heard the alarm, and did not inform the local personnel who had cooperated in handling the Qingxiang self-defense on weekdays, and allowed the bandits to slaughter them without looking back? What crime did our people commit? This is what the people of Jiangxi hear the most and feel the most heartbroken. The past is over, so what more can be said? In the future, all rescue of the dead and wounded, and the peaceful gathering of the people, are hoped to be strictly assessed for the responsibility of the Jiangxi Provincial authorities, in order to save the remnants. This is the eighth thing that we are eager to petition for. (9) Please issue a clear order to exempt all taxes and miscellaneous donations in the bandit-affected areas. The places destroyed by the Communist bandits were during the autumn harvest. There is no production, so where do the taxes come from? After the recovery, we should first recruit the refugees and stabilize the villages. Issuing a clear order to exempt all taxes and miscellaneous donations is the most urgent task to win people's hearts. This is the ninth thing that we are eager to petition for. (10) Please send personnel to distribute emergency relief with the army to rescue the disaster-stricken refugees. The areas in Jiangxi that were attacked by the bandits were burned and looted extensively. They searched and extorted everything, so naturally there were empty houses and no one was not hungry. In addition, it is the end of the year and the weather is cold, and transportation is blocked. Orphans and widows are everywhere. The army is everywhere, although it can get out of the water and fire, it cannot treat the freezing and hunger. Please have mercy on the heavy disaster situation of the survivors after the robbery. With the great power of the government, send fair special personnel to distribute emergency relief with the army, so as not to die from killing, but from hunger and cold. And our central government diligently cares for the people, and has issued emergency relief in the war zone, and has also approved 100,000 yuan for Hunan. What about the hidden dangers in Jiangxi Province for several years, which have been discovered in a situation that cannot be cleaned up at once? This is the tenth thing that we are looking up and crying for. The above ten points are all the personal requirements of the Jiangxi people and the good policies that the country should take. Therefore, we dare not avoid the trouble and go to Beijing to petition. We hope that your government will have the intention of being hungry and drowning, and will show great benevolence and justice, and quickly examine and implement it. Then the 30 million elders in Jiangxi will be grateful for your virtue more than the nine tripods. We are extremely frightened and wait for your orders."

Hunanese People Urgently Request Chiang to Personally Suppress the Communist Bandits 83

▲The Communist bandits are more severe than Yan and Feng in three aspects▲There are four major drawbacks to the bandit suppression troops

Changsha Dispatch: The communist bandits in Hunan province have become increasingly rampant. After He Long, Kuang Jixun, and others invaded Nanhua in western Hunan, they also attacked Jin and Li counties. Kong Hechong, Li Shixing, Huang Gonglue, and others in eastern Hunan have entrenched themselves in Pingjiang, occasionally advancing towards Changsha. In recent days, they have been fighting with Tao Guang's 31st Division and Hou Pengqi's Brigade of the 15th Division in the areas of Shasha'ao and Genggutai. In Liuyang, Zhang Jingwu's gang has spread to the northern, southern, and eastern parts of the county, attacking the city from time to time. Chaling has already been captured by Chen Shao's bandit gang. Anren was just recovered by Duan Heng, the Southern Hunan Garrison Commander, on the 7th. Youxian is also under siege by communist bandits, and He Jian is mobilizing a large army to provide assistance. Furthermore, intelligence indicates that Peng and Huang's large force is about to return to their old nests in Pingjiang and Liuyang, and that part of Zhu and Mao's forces may also enter Chaling and Youxian, bypass southern Hunan, and go to western Hunan to liaise with He, Kuang, and other bandits. Therefore, the people of Hunan province are extremely panicked and urgently hope that Commander-in-Chief Chiang will dispatch a large army to personally oversee the suppression. The Hunan Post-Disaster Relief Committee recently appointed Huang Zhenyuan as its representative, along with representatives from various public legal organizations, Zhou Jiezhi, to jointly go to Nanjing to petition the Fourth Plenary Session and Commander-in-Chief Chiang for a swift suppression of the bandits. The letter presented to Commander-in-Chief Chiang is extremely earnest and is transcribed as follows: "We believe that the founding of the Party and the country has been fraught with difficulties and dangers. The Gui rebellion had barely been quelled when Yan and Feng rebelled in succession, and the communist bandits took the opportunity to stir up trouble in the southeast. Fortunately, Your Excellency personally led the punitive expedition against Yan, Feng, and other rebels, and victory has been declared. Logically speaking, these communist bandits alone should not be difficult to subdue. However, these bandits are under the command of the Third International. Since joining our Party in the thirteenth year of the Republic, they initially pretended to use the name of our Kuomintang to instill their communist ideology. Later, they openly plotted to seize the Party's leadership and attempted to turn our entire country red. Their hideous faces have been clearly exposed. Our central government had no choice but to take measures to eliminate the communists. However, the more they were eliminated, the more they grew in number, and today they have become a widespread and difficult-to-eradicate force. Compared to Yan, Feng, and other rebels, they are truly incomparable. We respectfully submit this to Your Excellency. Yan and Feng destroyed unity and willingly became leaders of the rebellious forces, still using the guise of propriety to scheme for a time. The communist bandits, on the other hand, spread their heresies throughout the country, poisoning young students and enticing ignorant farmers and workers. Even in remote and poor villages, they are brewing uprisings. Occasionally, when they are captured and dealt with according to national law, they still shout slogans at the time of execution. The depth of their venom is much greater than that of Yan and Feng. Yan and Feng occupied the northwest provinces, imposing exorbitant taxes and levies, and disregarding the hardships of the people, which was still the normal behavior of warlords. The communist bandits, on the other hand, are extremely fierce and cruel, and have no humanity. In recent years, the massacres in Guangzhou, Hailufeng, Changsha in Jiangxi, and parts of Hubei, Anhui, Fujian, Sichuan, Zhejiang, Henan, Jiangsu, and Shandong provinces have been ravaged by them. Most of the cities have been reduced to ashes, and the villages have become ruins. The division of fields and burning of contracts in Hunan and Jiangxi, the conscription of men and confiscation of property, the seizure of wives for mixed marriages, and the establishment of schools to promote communism are even more shocking to hear. The intensity of their harm is also much greater than that of Yan and Feng. Although Yan and Feng had hundreds of thousands of soldiers, their momentum was greater than that of ordinary enemies. However, when confronting and fighting, they still did not lose the norms of military action. Therefore, once defeated, they would immediately disintegrate. The communist bandits, on the other hand, avoid the strong and attack the weak, and their movements are erratic. Wherever they go, local ruffians follow suit, and honest farmers are coerced. Like weeds in the spring breeze, they spring up everywhere. Therefore, each force, such as the Red Army, the Red Guards, and the Black Killing Squad, claims to have tens of thousands of men. According to various investigations, the communist bandits currently have more than 70,000 rifles, more than 600 machine guns, more than 6,000 pistols, and no fewer than 100 artillery pieces and mortars. The bandits' schemes are very cunning, and the bandits' strength is increasing. The difficulty of suppressing them is even greater than that of Yan and Feng. Since they are so deeply venomous, so intensely harmful, and so difficult to suppress, and considering the bandit suppression troops from all sides, there are several major drawbacks. Whenever bandit alarms are heard, temporary dispatches are made, each with its own circumstances, and must be carefully discussed. By the time the troops are mobilized, the bandits have already heard the news and fled far away, delaying the opportunity. This is the first drawback. The bandits' nests are mostly located in border areas. If they win, they loot everywhere. If they lose, they retreat with their loot. Our troops, even if they track and pursue them, will eventually return to their own province as soon as they cross the border, and the other province has no troops to attack in coordination. The boundaries are distinct, and the problem is allowed to fester. This is the second drawback. The troops from various routes do not cooperate with each other. Although one person is responsible for command, due to the distinction between host and guest, every order still needs to be approved. The army lacks discipline and is not conducive to military operations. This is the third drawback. The punitive expeditions against rebels are rewarded and punished by the state. If there are losses, they can be replenished at any time. The suppression of communist bandits is the sole responsibility of the local authorities. If they win, there is nothing special. If they lose, they can cover it up. Even if the losses are too great, they will disappear without a trace. Without a way to encourage and deter, who would be willing to sacrifice themselves? This is the fourth drawback. In short, the communist bandits are regarded as insignificant, so it is said that they are easy to annihilate. They do not know that the Yellow Turbans caused chaos in the Han Dynasty, and the roving bandits eventually led to the fall of the Ming Dynasty. Disaster lies in secrecy, and failure lies in negligence. Moreover, the communist bandits have become a force, and now take Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi as their central region. Their goal is to connect with the bandits in eastern Sichuan, southern Henan, northern Guangdong, southern Fujian, western Zhejiang, and northern Anhui to turn the Yangtze River basin red. In this regard, the trouble with Yan and Feng is just a minor ailment, while the communist bandits are a worry in the heart. Now that the minor ailment has been removed, but the worry in the heart remains. Even if there are plans for encirclement and suppression, there is no hope of realization. If it comes to the point where there is no other choice but to try to save the situation, it is known that with many troops and generals, there is no need to worry about defeat. However, military success takes time and will first demand many innocent lives. Hunan will become a bandit's haven, and there will be no survivors. We humbly believe that Your Excellency has received the heavy entrustment of the late Premier and is dedicating yourself to the Party and the country. Both at home and abroad, you are respected. Regarding Yan, Feng, and other rebels who shook the foundation of the country, you resolutely launched a punitive expedition and finally won the victory of the Three Principles of the People. You should not tolerate these communist bandits who openly sell out their country and are enemies of the Kuomintang. Therefore, we earnestly implore you to make a decisive decision, personally lead the victorious army of the punitive expedition, and implement the order to encircle and suppress them, so that the chief culprits and arch-criminals can be wiped out as soon as possible, so that the southeastern provinces can celebrate their revival, and the foundation of the country can be consolidated. In addition to sending representatives Huang Zhenyuan to come and pay respects and personally present everything, is there anything appropriate in the reasons for urgently requesting a personal expedition to the communist bandits in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces? We respectfully request that you examine and approve it for implementation." (November 9)

Local Dispatches

▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲▲

Suzhou 84

The Case of Han Jinshi's Unclear Death Takes an Unexpected Turn: The case of Han Jinshi, the wife of Han Youjiu of the Gejia Lane in the Lvmen neighborhood, whose death was unclear, was reported to the Wudi Court by her nephews, Han Guoduo and Han Guolin, who alleged that it was conspired by the evil servant Shi Junqing and Chen Li, Han Youjiu's aunt. However, the autopsy revealed no fatal injuries. The Han brothers were detained and counter-charged with the crime. The initial judgment was three years of imprisonment for each of them. After appealing to the High Court, the sentence was reduced to one year and eight months of imprisonment. The Han brothers, dissatisfied with the judgment, appealed to the Supreme Court and filed a petition with the National Government, accusing Lai Gan, the prosecutor of the Wuxian District Court, and the lawyer Hu Shikai of colluding to engage in corruption and shielding criminals and framing good people. Chairman Chiang, upon receiving the petition, immediately forwarded it to the Civil Service Department for consultation with the Judicial Yuan and ordered the Ministry of Justice to investigate. After reviewing and verifying the matter, Acting Minister Zhu issued an order yesterday (the 15th) to Wang Simao, the Chief Prosecutor of the High Court, to thoroughly investigate and handle the case.

Crab Boat Robbed by Bandits: Lu Hongfu, a villager from Beida Village, Taozhuang Town, Jiashan County, Zhejiang Province, and his wife and five others caught more than 600 catties of crabs in Zhujiajiao, Qingpu, and loaded them into 31 baskets. They were sailing to Suzhou to sell them when, at 6:00 PM, they passed Dushuhu Lake outside Fengmen Gate. Suddenly, they encountered a bandit boat with four bandits armed with pistols and single-edged knives. They intercepted Lu's boat and robbed 26 baskets of crabs, weighing 586 catties, as well as clothes, silver dollars, and other items, worth more than 300 yuan in total. After the bandits fled, Lu Hongfu sailed to Suzhou that night and reported the robbery to the Third District of the Water Police, requesting a manhunt.

Huai'an Assessor Accused: Guo Weiran, an assessor of the Huai'an County Government, was recently accused by Gao Shaomen and other citizens of the county in a petition to the High Court, accusing him of bending the law for personal gain, being corrupt, smoking opium, visiting prostitutes, accepting bribes publicly, and having a notorious reputation. They requested that investigators be sent to thoroughly investigate and punish him. After receiving the petition, the High Court ordered the county magistrate to thoroughly investigate and report back for verification yesterday (the 15th).

Tianye Conference Sets Rent Grain Price: The Tianye Public Association investigated the market price of rough japonica rice in various rice shops in the city this year and determined that the highest price was around nine yuan and five jiao. Therefore, it convened a meeting of various warehouse owners yesterday to discuss the price conversion. It was decided that each stone would be limited to nine yuan, and a reduction of 25% would be granted in accordance with the order, and no excess was allowed.

Jinshan 85

A Wave of Banditry Sweeping Jinshan: The bandit atmosphere in the southern part of Jinshan County has become increasingly rampant recently. Liujia Yanqiao is where TaiBao AShu established his gang, so many bandits gather there. Other small towns such as Qianjia Xu, Qingdui An, Wanchun Qiao, Li Jialangxia, Nanlu, Dianxia Qiao, and Gaojia Qiao are also frequently visited by these people because they are very close to Liujia Yanqiao. From then on, a piece of pure land was completely transformed into a bandit world. Recently, it was heard that more than 30 bandits from Situan, Pudong, carrying four mobile machine guns and dozens of long and short guns, arrived at Liujia Yanqiao a few days ago to negotiate with Taibao Ashu, willing to join the gang. Tang Meisheng, the patrol chief of the Qianjiaxu Public Security Bureau, and the police officer Jin Qisheng (the younger brother of the notorious bandit Jin Fei) have been in contact with the bandits, so they did not resist when the bandits came to rob them, and later joined the gang. Even more unemployed vagrants have joined, so the gang's power has grown, and they are becoming more blatant and tyrannical. The recent cases are listed below: (1) Several bandits came to He Haoyong's house northwest of Jieli An at dusk the other day, rushed in and robbed them. Haoyong's wife tried to escape through the back window but was shot and killed by the guarding bandit. (2) After robbing He Haoyong's house, the bandits went to Shen Xiaomao's house southwest of Jiaolili An to demand bandit funds. It is said that they had previously received a letter from the bandits asking to borrow 2,000 yuan of silver. Xiaomao was unable to pay and had repeatedly broken his promise, angering the bandits, so they set fire to his house, which spread to the Zhou family next door, destroying more than a dozen houses and killing a Zhou family's ox. (3) Several bandits came to Ye Yunxiang's house in Qitu, southwest of Gan An, on the 8th of this month to demand bandit funds. Yunxiang was also unable to pay and had already escaped. Unexpectedly, Yunxiang's younger brother did not have time to escape and was immediately shot and killed by the bandits. (4) A Shen surnamed man south of Liujia Yanqiao was killed by bandits on the 10th of this month because he had a feud with them. In addition, Jin Quan jing's house in Fangtangjing, Shen Chuangen's house north of Qianjiaxu, and the Zhang family in Mapengtou have also been robbed one after another, suffering heavy losses. It is also said that the bandits held a meeting a few days ago and decided that all township chiefs in each township must pay 1,000 yuan in bandit funds. Those within the bandit's territory have now received a notice from the bandits. As for sending letters to various families to extort loans, it is heard everywhere and is difficult to describe in detail. With the approaching winter, the bandit disaster continues, and people from all walks of life are worried. Therefore, the southern township must have bandit suppression troops stationed there.

Jiading 86

Settling the Account of Former County Magistrate Qian: Qian Baohe, the former county magistrate, suddenly left Jiading after the revolutionary army arrived. Two subsequent county magistrates, Chen and Ma, have not yet settled the account. Now, upon the strict urging of the provincial government, Qian sent Bao Yunyu as a representative to Jiading a few days ago. On the 14th, the Finance Bureau invited the Real Estate Department, the Education Bureau, and other departments to discuss the matter. Because the account books were not yet ready, it was necessary to schedule another meeting to calculate the land tax reduction of 14%. This year's cotton harvest is only 20% to 50% of the normal year. The disaster is even more serious in the eastern townships, where cotton accounts for 80% and rice accounts for 20%. Previously, the Provincial Department commissioned an investigation and determined that the entire county should be reduced by 78% and reported it to the province. Later, the provincial order did not approve it. The county government then proposed an 81% reduction to the province. Now, upon instruction, it has been decided to reduce the first district by 6%, the second district by 15%, the third district by 21%, the fourth district by 4%, the fifth district by 31%, the eighth district by 5%, and the sixth and seventh districts will not be reduced. The entire county will be reduced by 14%.

Wuxi 87

A Bizarre Murder Case in the Western Suburbs: The Rong family behind the Xinchun Tea Garden in the western suburbs of this county lives with Chen Shenshi, a 45-year-old woman from Jiangyin. Her husband, Chen, passed away 25 years ago, leaving behind a son named Jiabao, 25 years old, who is currently working on a drainage machine boat in Jiangyin's countryside. After her husband passed away, Chen Shenshi remarried Zhou Baoda, also from her hometown. Zhou works in a yarn factory in Jiangyin, but he does not come to Wuxi often, so Chen Shenshi, feeling lonely, became acquainted with Mao Ajin, a 25-year-old bathhouse attendant from Danyang. To avoid gossip, Chen Shenshi and Mao Ajin called each other "adopted mother" and "adopted son." This relationship had been going on for several years. The other night, Mao Ajin again stayed at Chen Shenshi's place. However, at 5:00 AM the next day (the 15th), Mao Ajin suddenly put on his clothes and hurriedly left. The landlord, the Rong family, saw this and became suspicious. They went upstairs to Chen Shenshi's bedroom to ask what was going on. Unexpectedly, Chen Shenshi was lying stiff on the bed, unresponsive. She had already died. The Rong family was shocked and immediately sent someone to Dongxin Road outside Guangfu Gate to report to the deceased's younger sister, Gu Shenshi. Upon hearing the news, she immediately rushed to her sister's house and mourned over the body. At the same time, she sent a telegram to Jiangyin to notify the deceased's husband, Zhou Baoda, and her son, Chen Jiabao, to come to Wuxi to handle the funeral. She also sent people to search for Mao Ajin, but his whereabouts were unknown. At noon, the ward head, Chen Zizhao, reported the matter to the county government and requested an autopsy. It is heard that the family plans to request the county government to waive the autopsy. The Culprit of the Bloodshed Incident at Beizhhaikou is Arrested: Zeng Haishan, a guest resident in No. 12 of the Junzi Workshop in Beizhhaikou, was suddenly attacked by thugs armed with knives at 1:30 AM on the 7th. Zeng's head and other parts of his body were slashed more than 20 times. The thugs immediately fled. Afterwards, Zeng Haishan was admitted to the Brothers Hospital for treatment, and his injuries are improving. However, Zeng's concubine, Yao Laoer (from Jiangyin), is suspected of knowing something about Zeng's murder. She has been detained by the Public Security Bureau and sent to the county government for questioning. At the same time, the police are closely investigating the thugs. Recently, Tan Baorong (working as a tea attendant at the Qitai Inn), a friend of Zeng Haishan, learned that the culprit in this case was indeed Sun Kundao, Yao Laoer's lover, who is now hiding in the Jiangnan Inn in Jiangyin. Therefore, yesterday (the 15th), he took a boat to Cheng and reported to the Jiangyin County Public Security Bureau, requesting an arrest. The bureau's detective team, accompanied by the informant Fan Xingbao, went to the Jiangnan Inn to search and arrested Sun Kundao in room No. 9. He was immediately taken to the bureau and transferred to the county government. At the same time, the county government was notified to send police to Cheng to escort him back for interrogation.

The Robbery Case on Tonghui Road is Cracked: The area along Hou Qi Street on Tonghui Road is notoriously remote, and robberies often occur. After 10:00 PM the other night, Sun Jingfu, a boatman living in Taosha Lane, was walking through the area when he was suddenly attacked by four thugs who robbed him of his clothes, two silver dollars, and dozens of copper coins. Sun immediately told the nearby night school students, who reported it to the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau. Zhou, the branch chief, dispatched three police officers to investigate and arrested Wang Xingbao, Chen Ziqing, and Chen Jian on the spot. The stolen goods were found on their bodies. After questioning them at the bureau, they were transferred to the county court for prosecution yesterday.

A Major Kidnapping Case in Xishan, Dongting: According to reports from the Second District of the Water Police in Wuxi, TaiBao Ashu, the leader of the Henan bandits in Taihu Lake, has recently gathered his remaining gang and is about to make trouble in the lakeside area. Chief Mao, upon receiving the report, was about to dispatch police to encircle and suppress them. According to another report, the home of Ma Wenxiang, a resident of Houbao Town in Xishan, Dongting, was looted by lake bandits the other night, with losses of about 1,000 taels of silver. Before leaving, they kidnapped Ma Wenxiang and his son Yuekui. Chief Mao, upon receiving the report, immediately ordered the Eighth Team under his command to quickly encircle and suppress them. Yang Ku Hang's boat was robbed on the way: Yang Ku Hang's boat travels between Yang Ku and Wuxi every day, carrying passengers and cargo, and its business is good. The other day, when it was sailing from Yang Ku to Wuxi, it suddenly encountered a pirate ship near Baitangxu. Eight or nine pirates, carrying pistols, flashlights, and other weapons, jumped onto the boat and opened fire as a warning. They immediately overturned the cabin and robbed everything. None of the passengers were spared. After half an hour, they left with their loot in the original boat. After an inspection, the total loss was more than 100 yuan. It was reported to the county yesterday, requesting an investigation.

Changzhou 88

The River Bridge Murder of Her Husband: Zhao Quangen of Zhao Jia Lane near the River Bridge in the Second District of Wu County married a woman named Zhang, who bore him a son. They were usually harmonious, but Zhang recently had an affair with her husband's uncle, Zhao Xiaolin, and saw her husband as an eyesore. On the morning of the 7th of this month, while her husband was fast asleep, she colluded with a field hand and a kiln maid to strangle him with a hemp rope. The next day, she claimed that he had committed suicide by hanging and hastily bought a coffin for burial in the field. Afterwards, her nephew, Zhao Guoming, and neighbor, Cai Changming, discovered the inside story and reported it to the county court on the 14th. After questioning the plaintiff, the prosecutor led the staff to the countryside on the morning of the 15th to open the coffin for an autopsy.

Robbery and Assault Case in the Second District: Jiang Jicheng's home in Jiangjia Village, Xinshu Township, Second District of Wu County, was suddenly robbed on the night of the 13th. Jiang Jicheng and his elderly mother were beaten all over and unable to move. Silver dollars, clothes, and ornaments were looted. Afterwards, the township head reported the case on their behalf.

Changshu 89

Suspicious Points Arise in the Cigarette Boat Robbery: Zhao Shouxin, a salesman from the Xincheng Cigarette Factory on Tangshan Road in Shanghai, came to Changshu to sell cigarettes. He was robbed in Niujing, at the border between Kunshan and Changshu. It is now heard that after Zhao was robbed, he reported to various armed agencies in Changshu and telegraphed the company in Shanghai. After receiving the report, the company sent Qian Yunping, a special commissioner, to Changshu to investigate and inquire at the Public Security Bureau and other places. It is now heard that Qian is paying close attention to the investigation. He now believes that Zhao's robbery was fraudulent and that there are many suspicious points. It may be related to Zhao's embezzlement, falsely claiming that he was robbed by bandits. At that time, he immediately reported the investigation to the factory by long-distance telephone for instructions. He has now ordered the two to return to Shanghai together for a final decision.

Summary of the County Government Meeting: The County Government of this county held its 29th county government meeting yesterday, chaired by County Magistrate Tan, with Secretary Jin acting as his proxy. The resolutions are summarized as follows: 1. Regarding the first phase of construction bonds issued by the Provincial Government, this county has been assigned a quota of 90,000 yuan. Regarding the method of raising funds, it was decided to refer to the method of handling customs treasury bills. 1. The Director of the Construction Bureau proposed that the situation of the county's ships is complex and that they should be reorganized by conducting ship registration, referring to the methods of Wuxi, Shanghai, and other counties. It was decided to revise and pass the ship regulations. 1. Regarding the old Bai Grain Warehouse, which was estimated by the Director of the Real Estate Department, the result was that the detailed accounts of the estimate were handed over to the Construction Bureau for quick review and reply because the previously submitted estimate has increased.

Jiangyin 90

Patient Dies from Wrong Prescription: Xue, the 51-year-old widow of the late Wu Heshu of Nanzha Street, suddenly suffered from liver wind entering the collaterals the other day. She hired Jiang Junpu, a doctor from this street, to treat her. Zhou Dexiu's daughter, Sanmei, 18 years old, from Hexi, also suffered from a deficiency and also hired Jiang to treat her. Unexpectedly, when the two families went to the Nanshoutang Pharmacy to fill their prescriptions, the owner, Su Baojun, mistakenly mixed up the two families' prescriptions and gave them to the people picking up the medicine, causing them to take the wrong medicine after returning home. Wu's wife, Xue, died in the middle of the night, and Sanmei is also in danger. Because the properties of the medicines are different, they are still in negotiations. The Chinese Medicine Association and the Health Association of this county also expressed their condolences yesterday, lamenting the lives of seriously ill people.

Yangzhou 92

Chicken and Duck Boat Sinks, Drowning People: At around 6:00 PM on the 12th, a chicken and duck transport boat of the Dada Transport Company was approaching the shore at Tie Niu Wan, Shaobo, when a pig boat coming straight from upstream crashed into the chicken boat. The owner of the chicken boat, Ge Chuanjin, and the boat crew Gao Xiaoer were knocked into the water. Ge was rescued, but Gao was swept away by the waves and died. The pig boat's owner, Liu Diankui, and the boatman Xu Laoer, were detained and sent to the Eighth Branch of the Public Security Bureau for questioning.

Landowners of the Airfield Demand Land Rent: The site of the Yangzhou Airfield was signed by the Provincial Security Department as the vacant land next to Puqing Palace outside Dongguan. It is now heard that the landowners of the airfield have stopped farming since the 16th year of the Republic when the official office designated it as an airfield. They announced that the rent was one yuan per mu, totaling more than 400 mu, which has not been paid for four years, totaling more than 1,600 yuan. In addition, there are several graves. Therefore, Chen Yuchao and others were publicly elected to petition the province to issue the owed rent. Yesterday (the 13th), the provincial government ordered the county to first survey and use the public land.

Inspection of Saltpeter and Sulfur Leads to Assault and Detention: Yin Xuecheng, Wang Bohua, Shu Yunyuan, Pang Zhuzhai, and other employees of the Saltpeter and Sulfur Inspection Office assaulted Wang Changming at his home in Erwei yesterday while inspecting saltpeter and sulfur. Because of a disagreement, the inspectors used force and injured Wang. The patrol team of the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau arrived at the scene and found two six-shot revolvers and five bullets on the inspectors, as well as a written order from Zhang Zidan, the director of the office. They were all taken to the bureau and have now been transferred to the headquarters for handling.

Shaoxing 93

Arbitration Committee to Mediate Tenancy Disputes: The Shaoxing Tenancy Arbitration Committee, in order to prevent disputes arising from the fact that the new tenancy agreements have not yet been agreed upon by both parties of the tenancy while the rice harvest in various townships is imminent, has considered using a notice form to notify the landowners to estimate the crops in the field. This method has been requested for instruction from the Provincial Arbitration Committee. Now, because it is not easy for tenants to prepare written notices, the interim measures for tenants to reduce rent by 25% originally intended for both parties of the tenancy to negotiate new tenancy agreements, as the legislative intent is to enforce them. If the power is really strong, there is no need for both parties to calculate the actual amount received in the field. It has now been decided that the county will distribute new tenancy agreement papers to each village, urging both parties to negotiate and sign them to ensure compliance and avoid disputes.

Provincial Order to Ban Private Credit Bureaus: The Shaoxing County Government received a provincial order yesterday to ban private credit bureaus. The five articles of the method of registering and obtaining licenses for private credit bureaus have now been issued to all bureaus for compliance.

Qiu Family of Xinshi Town Abducted by Bandits: At Xiatang, about three miles from Xinshi Town, farmer Qiu Bao-yuan's family is not wealthy; they make a living by farming. Pinghu 95

Increased Bounty for Bandit Leader Tai Bao A-Shu: Eastern Township bandit leader Tai Bao A-Shu has been rampant for a long time, and the people have suffered greatly. The provincial government previously offered a reward of one thousand yuan, strictly ordering the troops to apprehend him as soon as possible, but to no avail. Recently, the provincial government considered that the failure to capture this bandit has a significant impact on public security, so it specially convened a meeting and, in addition to the original reward of one thousand yuan, added a substantial reward, strictly limiting the time for his capture.

Ningbo 96

Warship Captures Twelve Pirates: On the 11th of this month, a large Fujian ship was sailing near Jinqing Port in the Dinghai waters when it suddenly encountered a pirate ship, which opened fire as a warning. The large ship was also equipped with firearms and resisted. Unable to get close, the Sui Nan warship happened to be passing by. Hearing the gunfire, it knew that pirates were robbing and immediately stopped to assist the large ship, surrounding the pirate ship and capturing thirteen pirates, rescuing two refugees. After the pirates were captured, they were escorted by the warship to the Dinghai Public Security Bureau and then transferred to the court for investigation.

Head of Education Section Resigns, New Appointment: The head of the Education Section of the Ningbo Municipal Government has resigned. Due to the municipal government's financial difficulties and the difficulty in handling affairs, many people are unwilling to serve as the head of the section. Since Yang Ziyi became mayor, the position has changed hands three times. It is now learned that the head of the section, Miao Ruizhi, has again submitted his resignation. Mayor Yang has appointed Hu Dafu, a staff member of the section, to fill the vacancy.

Two Abducted Girls Redeemed: A report stated that A-Yu, the second daughter of Wang Heqing of No. 5 Kaiming Lane in Ningbo, and Wang's three-year-old niece were abducted by bandits using trickery on the afternoon of the 1st of this month. It is now learned that after the bandits abducted A-Yu and the others, they sent letters to Wang's family twice. Wang went to Shanghai to negotiate with the bandits and redeemed them. Yesterday morning, Wang returned to Ningbo with his daughter A-Yu and the others. They took a train back to their ancestral home in Cibei that day.

Hangzhou 97

Inspection Measures for Transporting Rice Out of the Province: The Shanghai Municipal Government petitioned the Executive Yuan to order the Zhejiang Province to abolish the ban on the export of rice, in order to promote mutual circulation. The Zhejiang Provincial Government ordered the Department of Civil Affairs to discuss and respond. Yesterday, Director Cheng of the Department of Civil Affairs responded, stating that the province has not promulgated a ban on the export of rice but has clearly allowed people to transport it freely. Without inspection, the province's grain supply would lose its basis for regulation. Therefore, it is proposed that merchants and people transporting rice out of the province for sale must first submit the quantity and location, and attach a guarantee that they will be responsible for transporting rice in case of shortage. The local government will then issue a passport. Merchants and people from outside who purchase from Zhejiang Province must have their local government consult with the government of the purchasing location to verify and issue a permit. All permits must be submitted to the local customs and police for inspection and release in order to facilitate inspection.

Provincial Government Sends Troops to Suppress Fujian Bandits: Although the major threat of Fujian bandits in Zhejiang Province has passed, the remaining bandits have not yet been completely eliminated. The Zhou Yuguang gang of Taishun County recently showed signs of infiltrating Qingyuan County. In addition to jointly suppressing them with Fujian Province, the provincial government yesterday telegraphed Liu Xiyi, the commander of the First Regiment, to make thorough defense preparations and report on the defense situation.

Mrs. Baillou to Fly to Beijing Tomorrow, Then to Jinan 99

▲ Checking the Machinery ▲ Attending Various Banquets

British aviator Mrs. Baillou, after arriving in Shanghai the other day, is scheduled to depart from Hongqiao Airport at 6:00 AM on Monday, weather permitting. She will first fly to the capital, stay for a while to refuel, and then continue to Jinan for the night before crossing the sea to Seoul, Korea, and then crossing the Sea of Japan to Tokyo. However, the section from Seoul to Tokyo is currently under Japanese autumn maneuvers, and civilian aircraft are prohibited from flying over the maneuver area, so it may be delayed for a few days before she can complete the trip. Mrs. Baillou originally planned to leave Shanghai on Sunday, but when she checked the machinery yesterday morning, she found damage, so she stayed in Shanghai for one day to repair it. The oil tank inside the aircraft suddenly leaked. Initially, it was wrapped in leather, but it did not seem to be effective. She has now purchased rubber wrapping material in Shanghai, which should prevent oil leakage. Mrs. Baillou was very busy with social engagements in Shanghai yesterday (the 15th). She went to Hongqiao Airport to check the machinery at 9:30 AM in the morning, then attended a welcome banquet hosted by the Shanghai Women's Association Joint Committee at noon, a tea party hosted by the British Women's Association in the evening, and a banquet hosted by the Royal Air Force Veterans Association at night. According to Mrs. Baillou, she plans to travel around the world by plane. After arriving in Japan, she plans to take the Japanese Empress ship to the United States, first flying to New Albany, Indiana, to visit her mother's old home. Mrs. Baillou's mother is American, and her grandfather participated in the American Civil War and made contributions. Mrs. Baillou also intends to reside in the United States in the future. After flying to New Albany, she plans to continue to New York and then visit various countries in North and South America before taking a ship to Africa, flying along its coast back to Europe and England.

Important News from the Yangtze River Shipping Industry 103

▲ Continued Release of Merchant Ships: After the end of military operations, the central government continued to rent more than ten merchant ships to Pukou for transporting bandit suppression troops into Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan provinces, and then distributed the various divisions to the ports of Xunhan. Recently, the transport will be completed. In order to restore the river and sea shipping industry, various shipping companies have sent representatives to Beijing to request the Ministry of Communications to release the ships. Yesterday, this port received a telegram from Beijing stating that all of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Yangtze River ships, except for the Jiangtian, have been released. Now, the Fair Winds and Prosperous Voyages and other sea ships have also been released and will arrive in Shanghai today. The Changxing of the Sanbei Company has also been ordered to be released and should be fully returned to Shanghai in about a week. Jianghai Hualun can be fully restored to service in the near future.

▲ Changsha Navigation: The Changsha route of the Chinese merchant ships has been suspended for a long time. This time, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company appointed Li Yunliang to Wuhan to reorganize the Yangtze River shipping industry. Li has reported to Shanghai that the navigation rights in Hunan and Hubei have long been occupied by foreign merchants. A plan to recover and restore the route has now been drawn up. Starting in mid-November, the Changsha route will be restored, with five or six voyages per month, with one ship departing every five days. The Liyuan and Liji ships have been assigned to operate the route. Due to the shortage of ships, six large tugs have been chartered to operate as substitutes.

▲ Special Goods Can Be Loaded: The case of special goods from Sichuan being transported to Hunan and Hubei under official transport was negotiated by Li Muqing, the director of the Special Tax Bureau, with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, which agreed to use the Kuailli ship to transport them. The first shipment was transported from Sichuan on the 6th of this month. When passing through Yichang, it was detained by the Yichang Customs, which considered it to be smuggled local products and refused to allow it to be transported to Wuhan. The ship was also detained. Later, Li Muqing went to Yichang to explain the situation to the customs officials and tax commissioners before they allowed it to be transported to Hankou. The matter has now been resolved, and the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will begin transporting the goods later this month.

▲ Flying Tiger Difficult to Salvage: The Sanbei Company's Flying Tiger ship, after being sunk by a navy warship in the Yangtze River near Hankou on February 23 of this year, was entrusted to the Rongchangcheng Salvage Company in Shanghai for salvage. After many attempts, it was found that the ship was submerged in the riverbed and could not be salvaged. The ship had reported an insurance claim of 80,000 taels of water insurance. It is now reported that the insurance company believes that this case is an accident caused by military transport and does not meet the repair rules for ordinary claims and may refuse to pay the claim. The matter is currently being negotiated, but there is no hope for salvage.

Freight Car Derails on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Last Night 104

Around 9:00 PM last night, the No. 209 inbound freight train on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway derailed while passing through Danyang Station. Due to the excessive height of the heavy cargo loaded on the open car, a package of goods fell onto the track, causing two cars to derail and one to overturn as the train passed. Fortunately, no one was injured. The Changzhou Machine Factory was notified and dispatched a rescue train to help. It is reported that if the track damage is not significant, it can be repaired that night. Otherwise, the overnight express trains in both directions may be delayed as a result.

Tobacco Dealers Appeal for License Stamps 106

▲ Tax on Tax, Taxed Again

The Shanghai South Office of the Municipal Tobacco Dealers Association sent a letter to the Executive Committee yesterday, stating: "We are writing to inform you that we have received a letter from Wanchang Tobacco Shop, a member in Dongjiadu, stating that an inspector of stamp taxes confiscated a license paper on the 11th because they inadvertently failed to affix a stamp. It was not a deliberate violation. We are writing a special letter to request the authorities to be lenient, waive the penalty, and allow the license to be returned. We have also received letters from Committee Member Chen Kunxian, along with Defeng, Shunda, Hongda, and other members from Nine Acres, stating that after paying the annual license fees for tobacco products, the collection office did not issue formal licenses but only issued temporary receipts for the license fees. The receipts were stamped with a blue 'After investigating the business tax amount and finding it to be consistent, the formal license will be exchanged.' As a result, on the 9th, a stamp inspector mistakenly believed that these receipts were licenses that had not been deliberately stamped and detained them. The license tax was implemented during the warlord era and was a type of exaction. Stamps were not affixed. Previously, it was levied on locally produced water and drought tobacco. Our industry has long ceased to sell locally produced products and has stopped selling them for a long time. The cigarettes currently sold have already been subject to factory output tax and unified tax. Locally produced tobacco and alcohol have also been subject to public sale, landing, and license taxes. There are many types of taxes. Under the Qing Tian Bai Ri Party's rule, while abolishing exactions and miscellaneous taxes and relieving the people's suffering, the license tax should be exempted. At this moment, not only cannot the license tax be exempted, but stamps must also be affixed. For the temporary receipts for the license fees, stamps must also be affixed and then stamps must be affixed when the formal license is exchanged. This is truly taxing again and again, taxing on tax. Even if stamps must be affixed, they should be treated like invoices and receipts issued by customers to stores for purchases, so that the treatment is fair. All our tobacco, sundries, and grocery stores are small businesses, seeking meager profits and barely maintaining a living. At this time of rising prices and hardship, how can we bear this heavy burden? Therefore, we dare to state the facts and seek assistance, appealing to the authorities that, for the license stamps, during the period when the persuasion to affix is just beginning, it should be uniformly exempted, and all temporary receipts for the license fees that have been paid should be returned quickly so that they can be exchanged for formal licenses to ensure business and show compassion, etc., etc. We have received the letter and are copying it for your information, hoping that you will investigate and handle it."

Party and Government Agencies' Measures for Silk Workers 108

Previously, all silk factories in Shanghai closed down due to the exhaustion of capital losses. Subsequently, the Shanghai Silk Factory Association convened a general meeting, where Chairman Shen earnestly persuaded them to prioritize the livelihood of the workers. At that time, he promised to make efforts to resume work, etc. This has been reported in this newspaper several times. The Shanghai Municipal Party Department, the Municipal Public Security Bureau, the Bureau of Social Affairs, and other agencies have paid close attention to this matter. After receiving separate reports from labor and management, they sent personnel to various silk factories in the Hongkou District yesterday to conduct on-site investigations of workers. They learned that although the Workers' Union had convened a general meeting beforehand, the workers did not approve the proposal not to work. However, Chen Zongxiang temporarily forced the mechanics of nine silk factories to sign, prohibiting them from starting fires and not providing power, making it impossible for the factories to start work. Also, many well-behaved workers were suffering from the long-term work stoppage and had a good understanding of the factory's difficulties in sluggish sales and losses. They were willing to temporarily reduce wages and cooperate sincerely, hoping to restore the original situation once the silk market improved. After receiving the reports from the investigators, the Public Security and Social Affairs Bureaus immediately invited Chairman Shen of the Industry Association and Standing Committee Member Zhu Jing'an to the bureau for detailed inquiries in the afternoon. The situation of chaos at the time and the current situation of the majority of workers were consistent with the investigation reports. An order was immediately issued to severely punish the ringleaders who were detained. At the same time, the nine silk factories were ordered to start work immediately and increase the protection of the police. If anyone caused further trouble, they would be arrested by name.

National Products Association Receives Reply Telegram from the Ministry of Finance Regarding the Problem of Rubber Being Re-Taxed Upon Landing 112

The Chinese National Products Maintenance Association previously reported that the products of the member Dasheng Rubber Factory were being re-taxed upon landing when transported to Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and other provinces, hindering sales. They telegraphed the Ministry of Finance to order that the tax be waived according to the case. Yesterday, they received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance, stating: "(Omitted title) The association's telegram stating that the products of the Dasheng Rubber Manufacturing Factory were being re-taxed upon landing in Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and other provinces, requesting that the tax be waived according to the case, has been separately ordered by the Ministry to the finance departments of Hunan and Hubei provinces and the Jiangxi Finance Special Commissioner to investigate and forward orders to stop the practice and handle the matter according to regulations. A telegram was also sent to inform you. The Jiangxi Finance Special Commissioner, Liu Hao, reported that since Jiangxi Province abolished the unified tax and implemented the special consumption tax, the names of landing tax, etc., have long been abolished. If it is a machine-made imitation of foreign goods, which has been approved by the Ministry, the first customs bureau or the transit customs bureau will verify that the goods match the bill and exempt them from tax. The telegram from the Chinese National Products Maintenance Association stated that Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and other provinces were collecting landing tax, but Jiangxi Province did not have this item. It was also found that the factory had received an order from the Ministry on August 5 of this year regarding the factory name and trademark, which was forwarded to the Inland Consumption Tax Bureau for tax exemption according to regulations. Besides re-ordering the investigation, the Ministry should first submit a written report. The Secretary of the Association has transcribed the order for the Dasheng Factory to check."

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's Reply Regarding Responsibility for Business Collateral 120

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Chaozhou Sugar and Sundries Trade Association yesterday in response to inquiries regarding the responsibility for business collateral, stating: "In response to your letter of the 4th of this month, based on the request from member Jucheng Firm, seeking clarification on two points of doubt regarding the responsibility for business collateral, we promptly instructed the Commerce Department to dispatch personnel to investigate. The Commerce Department reported back stating, 'Regarding the case of investigating the customs of commodity collateral, we have now clarified the matter with all parties and recorded it as follows: (1) In the case where Party A uses white-made goods to obtain a loan from Party B, if the goods are not transferred to Party B, and the goods are lost or destroyed before redemption, who should be responsible? In principle, Party A should be responsible. (2) If Party A transfers the collateral to Party B, who should be responsible if the goods are lost or destroyed? In principle, Party B should be responsible. (3) Reasoning: The circulation of goods is inseparable from the creation, extinction, and transfer of the right to dispose of them and the responsibility for them. The responsibility for goods is determined based on the transfer of the above-mentioned rights. For example, when goods are used as collateral, the lender lends money to the owner of the goods, and the ownership of the goods should be transferred to the lender as security for the debt. The expression of this transfer is the transfer of the goods. If Party A is the owner of the goods and Party B is the lender, and Party A has a debt relationship with Party B but has not yet transferred the ownership of the goods (i.e., Party A's goods have not been transferred to Party B), then although Party B has obtained the claim, it has not obtained the ownership of the goods. Therefore, the responsibility for these collateral goods should naturally be borne by Party A. Conversely, if the goods have been transferred to Party B, then Party B has not only obtained the claim but also the ownership of the collateral. Since the ownership of the goods has been obtained, the responsibility for the goods should naturally be borne by Party B.' The above-mentioned investigation process is hereby reported, requesting your review and transfer to the relevant parties." Accordingly, a letter was drafted and sent in response, hoping that you will investigate, acknowledge, and inform the relevant parties accordingly. This is addressed to the Chaozhou Sugar and Sundries Trade Association in this city.
