Bloodshed in Changan Lane, Annakin Road 126

▲A Woman Died Horribly

▲Her Neck Was More Than Half Severed

▲There Was a Prostitute License Photo in Her Bag

▲The Deceased Appeared to Be a Prostitute

Yesterday morning, in front of house number 2, Changan Lane, 56 Annakin Road, French Concession, next to the north side of the Weiyang Grand Theater, a woman was found murdered with a knife. The deceased looked like a prostitute, and the circumstances were extremely bizarre. The detailed investigation is recorded below:

▲Second Landlord Xie Zidan Xie Zidan, a native of Zhenjiang, is 63 years old. He used to work in a cloth shop, but has been unemployed for more than ten years. He married a widowed woman, Chen Linshi, who is now 62 years old. Linshi has a son named Chen Dengyuan, who is 43 years old and works as an assistant in the kitchen of the Puyi Yarn Factory wholesale office on Nanjing Road. Dengyuan is married to a Yuan woman, who is 43 years old. The whole family lives at house number 3, Changan Lane, Annakin Road. In addition to living in house number 3, Xie Zidan's family also rented a single-family Shikumen house at number 2 in the same lane seven years ago, serving as a second landlord. However, the entire house at number 2 was sublet to three tenants, except for a Yangzhou maid, Wu Wangshi (44 years old), who lived in the loft and looked after the house. The front building of the house was rented to a He family who performed operas, the back building was rented to a chef, and the downstairs hall was rented to the Chen and Jin families. Another pavilion room was newly rented to a Zhang family from Pudong on the 6th of this month.

▲New Tenant Zhang A'er On the 1st of this month, a middle-aged couple, looking like husband and wife, came to rent the pavilion room at number 2, agreeing on a monthly rent of six yuan and paying a deposit of one yuan in advance. They moved in on the 6th. The Zhang family claimed to be named A'er and worked as a carpenter at the Huajie Waterworks Company. Their luggage was very simple, with only a bed, a table, and two chairs. After moving in, the woman asked Xie's maid, Wu Wangshi, to wash the chamber pot for them, agreeing to pay a small tip of five jiao per month. Wangshi did as she was told and washed it for them daily.

▲One Person Laying Face Up in Bed Yesterday at dawn, Wu Wangshi finished emptying Zhang's chamber pot and placed it on the left side of the pavilion room's door. At around 12:00 noon, Wangshi went upstairs for something and glimpsed the chamber pot, which was still outside the door. So she knocked on the door and called out repeatedly, but there was no response. However, when she exerted a little force, the door suddenly opened slightly, and the door was already locked. At first, she suspected that the couple had gone out together. When she peeked in carefully, she saw a person lying face up in bed, with both feet hanging down and the upper body covered by a curtain. She called out several more times, but there was still no response.

▲A Horrifying Decapitated Female Corpse When Wangshi saw that calling out did not elicit a response, she became suspicious. She ran to tell Xie's daughter-in-law, Yuan, and they went back together. They called out again, but still there was no response. So Xie ran to report to the Songshan Road Police Station. The chief of police heard the news and immediately ordered patrol officers to rush there. They unlocked the door and entered, and there was a horrifying decapitated female corpse lying across the bed. The deceased's head had been more than half severed, with only a piece of skin connecting the back of the head. The bloodstains were blurred, and the scene was unbearable to witness. The upper body was wearing a red striped cloth short shirt, and the lower body was naked. The hair had been cut off, and the feet were natural and barefoot.

▲What Was Seen at the Beef Shop A blood-stained pair of trousers was also found next to the bed. It seemed that the murderer had smeared the blood from the weapon on the trousers. Two beef noodle bowls and a porcelain basin were still on the table. The patrol officers went to the Yang Shunxing beef shop next door to inquire. According to the shop, a man came there around 1:00 AM and ordered two bowls of beef noodles. At around 2:00 AM, the man came again and ordered twenty beef pot stickers. The first time the noodles were delivered, the woman was seen supporting her chin with her hand, looking sad. The second time, the woman was lying across the bed, but she was still speaking as usual. It is estimated that the murderer committed the crime sometime after 3:00 AM.

▲The Deceased Appeared to Be a Prostitute After the patrol officers finished inspecting the scene, they notified the Tongren Fuyuan Hall mortuary and ordered a coffin bearer to go there and take the body to the mortuary to await autopsy. At the time, a prostitute license photo was found in the deceased's pocket. The face was the same as the deceased's. The photo was signed Li Shuangfeng, 25 years old, and was issued on October 9th of this year. The Pingkang Tongshan Association has sent people to investigate the truth. As for the details of how she died, it remains to be confirmed.

Gu Zhenxiang Has Been Kidnapped for Ten Months Without News 127

▲Kidnapped by Bandits at the Train Station ▲Numerous Attempts to Find Him Have Been Unsuccessful

▲The Bandits Have Not Sent a Ransom Demand

Gu Zhenxiang, a native of Jiashan, Zhejiang, is 44 years old. He used to be a member of the Zhejiang Provincial Assembly. In recent years, he has been engaged in the silk cocoon business. His financial situation is not affluent, but he is very generous and charitable. He has always had friendly relations with his friends and has never had any conflicts. He has a wife and children who depend on him for their livelihood. However, on the 27th day of the twelfth month of the lunar calendar last year, Gu left his hometown in the morning to catch the Shanghai-Hangzhou train due to business matters. He arrived in Shanghai at 12:00 noon. He immediately got off the train and walked out of the station, intending to hire a car to ride in. Unexpectedly, as soon as he left the iron gate, a car suddenly blocked his path, and three or four bandits jumped out, grabbed Gu, and shoved him into the car, which immediately sped away. At the time, a fellow villager of Gu's who was familiar with him saw this happen while traveling to Shanghai on the same train. After the fellow villager reported this to Gu's family, Gu's family came to Shanghai to find ways to investigate and reported the incident to various agencies, requesting their assistance in the investigation. Later, because there was no news, they published advertisements in various newspapers offering a reward for information. It is now learned that since Gu was kidnapped, his wife has been crying and his children have been weeping day and night, unable to stop. They are worried and anxious, and their situation is unbearably tragic. They thought that since he was kidnapped, there would be a ransom demand. Therefore, they stretched their necks and waited, day after day, but there was no news. It has been ten months, and there is still no news. Gu's family is still in a state of doubt, as they do not know whether Gu is alive or dead, and his wife is as anxious as ever. They sent someone to Shanghai again a few days ago, intending to find a way to investigate his whereabouts. However, after staying for several days, they could not find any information and had no way to start. That person took the train back to his hometown early yesterday morning.

Kidnapping and Escape of Hostages 128

▲Ten Rescued People Have Been Sent Back to Their Hometowns ▲Six Kidnapped People, Ransom Demanded: 150,000 Yuan

The Industrial Special Police Team stationed at the mouth of the Wusong River outside of the Hai Fu Town intercepted a bandit ship at the port on the morning of the day before yesterday at approximately 8:00 AM. The bandits had already escaped in advance. The police rescued ten hostages from the ship's cabin, including Zhang Xiafeng and Cai Xuewei, both male and female. They had all been kidnapped from places such as Yangzhou and were being held for a large ransom. They had been held for more than twenty days. Fortunately, they were rescued this time. The hostages were overjoyed. The hostages were then escorted back to their respective hometowns. However, at approximately 3:00 PM that afternoon, a large group of sea bandits suddenly arrived in the Lu Hongzha area of Haimen and kidnapped the owners of a certain wood shop and pig shop, totaling six people. The bandit ship is currently anchored in the Xiasha port of Haimen County. The bandits are demanding a total ransom of 150,000 yuan and have openly sent bandits to negotiate with the families.

Attempted Extortion, Falsely Accused as a Communist Party Member 129

▲Yu Renbiao Had Evil Intentions ▲Jiang Chunkai Nearly Suffered Because of Him

Jiang Chunkai, a native of Tongzhou, lives in Shanghai and makes a living as a road worker. He resides at 36 Huade Road. A few days ago, his fellow villager Yu Renbiao and a Yu man named Ma Wenlin suddenly came to Jiang's house, claiming to be detectives in the police station. They accused Jiang of being a communist party member and of committing two cases of murder and robbery in Tongzhou and said they were here to arrest him. If he wanted to avoid arrest, he would have to pay 800 yuan, otherwise, they would not let him go. Jiang knew that Yu was known for extortion and was not moved at all, so they started arguing. Jiang's sister-in-law Zhao Sunshi came out to help Jiang, but they even wanted to beat her. They left in anger. At 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, Ma Wenlin passed by Qiwupu Road and saw a Japanese detective from number 131 on patrol. He suddenly had an evil thought and reported to the detective that Jiang was a communist party member and asked him to arrest Jiang. The Japanese detective did not know the details and reported to the chief of police, who sent Chinese detectives Zhang Degong and others to arrest Jiang at his address. Jiang had not returned from work, and by the time Jiang returned, Yu Renbiao was following behind Jiang. The detectives arrested Jiang and Yu together and took them to the Yangshupu Police Station. After the chief of police inquired in detail, he realized that Jiang had been framed by Yu and Ma. Therefore, Jiang was released, and Yu was detained. The police were also ordered to arrest Ma. Yesterday, they were escorted to the Special Zone Local Court. Judge Feng Shide questioned them. Zhang Tianyin, the lawyer of the police station, stated that Ma Wenlin used to be a patrol officer at the Yangshupu Police Station with number 760, but he was dismissed for dereliction of duty. However, he did not repent and continued to recruit disciples. Yu Renbiao is one of his disciples and specializes in extortion. He has committed many crimes, and the police have wanted to arrest him for a long time. However, since he has committed many crimes, they still need to investigate them one by one, so he requested a postponement. Then, Jiang Chunkai accused Yu of asking to borrow two yuan from him, but he refused, so he invited his teacher to make up stories and frame him. Zhao Sunshi also stated that she was beaten and injured in the head and waist and had not fully recovered. When Yu was questioned, he only admitted to borrowing money from Jiang, but he denied everything else. Ma Wenlin said that Jiang was a communist party member and had committed crimes in his hometown. Everything was said by Yu's friend. He knew the Japanese detective because he was a patrol officer and knew the Japanese detective at number 131, so he reported to the Japanese detective. After the Japanese detective recounted the incident, Judge Feng ordered Yu and Ma to be detained and postponed the hearing to investigate the matter.

Trafficking a Large Quantity of Heroin on the Italian Ship "Illo" 130

The American Evening Post reports that customs officials continued to inspect cargo from Shanghai carried by the Italian ship "Illo" from Krakow today. They discovered over 300 pounds of pure heroin. Based on the current price of 20 US dollars per ounce, it is worth more than 336,000 Mexican dollars. The ship's cargo has not yet been fully inspected, and further discoveries are expected. Today's seized items consist of 220 tins and 40 bags, all concealed within dried fruit and other goods. The weight of each tin varies slightly, while each bag weighs one kilogram, approximately 2.5 pounds. The quantity of heroin seized in recent days is so large that it is feared to be unprecedented in the 70-year history of the Jianghai Customs. Customs officials are now planning to thoroughly inspect all incoming ships for any suspicion of carrying narcotics.

Trial of the Zhao Assassination Case Underway 131

▲Xia Admits to Being One of Those Who Conspired to Kill Zhao

Shen Jinghua, the head of the Shanghai County Public Security Bureau, personally went to Hefei in Anhui Province and apprehended Xia Shaoen, a suspect in the assassination of Zhao Tieqiao, a commissioner of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. After several days of interrogation by the bureau, a confession has been obtained. Xia has admitted to being one of the conspirators in the Zhao assassination and to being present at the Bund. Whether he personally killed Zhao is still under investigation. It is reported that once the interrogation is complete, the case will be reported to the county and submitted to the province for review. Yesterday, the Municipal Public Security Bureau sent personnel to retrieve Xia, but the transfer was not made as the interrogation is still ongoing.

Thorough Investigation of the Incident of a Japanese Guard Firing at Villagers at the Mitsui Coal Depot in Pudong 132

▲Having a Gun Doesn't Justify It ▲Luckily No One Was Hurt

The Mitsui Coal Depot in Yangjing, Pudong, built over 40 workshops during the May Thirtieth Movement to accommodate its workers. The workshops are separated from Caijiazhai village by only a Maqiao Stream. The villagers, numbering over 300 households, rely entirely on the water in this stream for drinking. Since the construction of the workshops, the workers have dug a trench next to the buildings, directly connecting to the stream, and all the dirty and unclean water is discharged into the stream through the ditch. The coal dust from the loading and unloading of coal at the depot is also discharged into the river, causing the clear water in the Maqiao Stream to become polluted. This not only hinders hygiene but also threatens the drinking water supply of the entire village. On the evening of the 8th, around 7 p.m., during a heavy rain, workers were again pouring polluted water into the river. Villagers from Caijiazhai came out to advise the workers to focus on hygiene, but the workers, relying on the power of the Japanese, refused to heed the advice, leading to a conflict. The Japanese guard of the Mitsui Coal Depot suddenly fired four shots at the villagers with a pistol. Fortunately, no one was injured. Cai Youxiang, the platoon leader of the 4th Platoon of the Caijiazhai Defense Corps, upon hearing the shots, immediately led the defense corps to investigate. It was then that he learned of the conflict between the villagers and the workers and that the Japanese guard had fired his pistol without authorization. Together with villager Huang Jiafu and others, they seized two of the unruly workers, one surnamed Zhang from Chongming and one surnamed He from Jiangbei, and took them to the Second Precinct of the Third District of the Public Security Bureau. Director Tang dispatched Patrol Officer Li to conduct an on-site investigation, and after understanding the situation, he met with Ishitaka, the Japanese manager of the coal depot. Ishitaka denied that the guard had fired the gun, claiming instead that the four shots were fired by the defense corps. He also issued a written statement to that effect. Director Tang has transferred the two workers and the Japanese manager's letter to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. Upon learning of this incident, the Japanese Consulate sent personnel to the Public Security Bureau, initially attempting to deny the incident, claiming that the coal depot guard did not carry a gun. However, after the Public Security Bureau produced a letter from Ishitaka admitting that the guard had a gun but did not fire it, the Japanese had no further argument. It is reported that the Japanese Consulate has requested the Public Security Bureau to conduct a thorough investigation of the case. If it is confirmed that the guard fired the gun, the case can be handed over for trial.

Two Barrels of Tung Oil Were Actually Opium Paste 133

Yesterday morning, around 8 a.m., Zhang Yushu, a patrol officer from the Second Squad of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol, was patrolling the Suzhou Creek near the Ponton Lane Bridge in the northern part of the city when he spotted a Xin Yong'an steamboat anchored there. He boarded the ship to conduct an inspection and found two asphalt barrels on deck, marked with the words "asphalt". As there was no one guarding them, he made inquiries but no one claimed ownership. He then inserted an iron skewer into the barrels and pulled it out, and suddenly smelled the scent of opium. Wondering why asphalt barrels would smell of opium, he became suspicious. He then devised a way to pry open the lids of the two barrels and carefully inspected the contents. They contained pure opium paste, estimated to be over 1,200 taels. He immediately took the evidence back to his squad and transferred it to the Nanshi Headquarters. After Director Xu inspected the items, he immediately prepared a document reporting the seizure of the two barrels of opium paste to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for further investigation.

Illegally Connecting Electrical Wires to Steal Electricity 134

▲Each Fined 50 Dollars

The Shanghai Municipal Council's Electricity Department discovered that Zhu Zhangshi at 1237 Jiaxing Road, Xin Luoshi at 1242 Jiaxing Road, and Yan Yuming at 1247 Jiaxing Road were illegally connecting electrical wires to their neighbors' homes to steal electricity, causing the public to suffer losses of over a hundred dollars. The relevant police station was notified, and the case was brought before the Special District Court. Yesterday morning, Judge Shen sentenced each defendant to a fine of 50 dollars. If they were unable to pay, they would be imprisoned for one day for every two dollars owed.

Visit to the Newspaper by Chinese and Foreign Dignitaries 136

▲Mr. Sro. J.R. Scherer, Special Representative of the Central Committee of the International Esperanto Movement, and His Colleague Mr. Sro. Slinger

Recently, Mr. Sro. J.R. Scherer, a special representative of the Central Committee of the International Esperanto Movement, and his colleague Mr. Sro. Slinger, came to Asia from the United States in September to inspect the state of Esperanto movements in various countries. They stayed in Japan for over a month, where they were warmly welcomed by their comrades. Mr. Scherer arrived in Shanghai on the 11th of this month and was received by representatives sent by the Shanghai Esperanto Society at 75 Hongji Lane, Baoshan Road, Zhabei, Shanghai. He gave a lecture at Fudan University the other day, with an audience of over 300 people. He gave a lecture at the Society the previous evening, showing slides. Yesterday, accompanied by Sun Yizhi and Pan Tishu, two members of the Shanghai Esperanto Society, he visited our newspaper office and had his photograph taken in our photography department. He praised all the facilities of our newspaper and said that he was very honored to see the oldest and largest newspaper in China. It is reported that Mr. Sro. Perraire, a Frenchman who is traveling around the world by bicycle and relying entirely on Esperanto, has recently arrived in China. He plans to travel to Zhenjiang and other places in the near future and then take a route through Guangzhou to the United States.

▲Students from Jiaotong University

Feng Yuzhang and other students from the Department of Political Economics of the Law School of the National Jiaotong University, more than 30 people, came to visit our newspaper office yesterday afternoon at 2 p.m., and were received by Mr. Huang Jiping, who showed them around various departments. They said goodbye and returned to school after an hour.

The Social Affairs Bureau Releases Suicide Statistics for September 137

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau released suicide statistics for September, stating that the number of suicide cases this month was 9 fewer than last month, totaling 173 cases. Among those who committed suicide due to marriage problems were aviator Wu Dehu and actress Mao Jianpei, both of whom took their own lives due to lack of freedom in marriage, which has attracted much social attention. Zhu Ruchao, representing the Zhejiang Provincial Bank, was robbed when he came to Shanghai last month to deliver funds, causing severe mental distress. He attempted suicide repeatedly, first by jumping into the Huangpu River, where he was rescued, and later by slitting his throat, a truly tragic situation.

Sandboat Robbed on the Qingkou Sea 139

▲Silver Dollars and Salted Pork Stolen ▲Many Crew Members Injured

The Beikou sandboat Jinde Yu sails to various ports in Dalian, Shandong, and specializes in carrying passengers and cargo back and forth. Last month, the ship left Shanghai and sailed to Dalian, carrying local cloth and other goods. After unloading the cargo in Dalian, it planned to carry soybean oil back to Shanghai. Because it had to wait for a specific date to load the cargo, the shipowner, Mr. Ling, thought that Shandong salted pork was being sold on the market and needed to be transported by boat, so he sailed to Qingkou, Shandong. He was hired by a merchant to load more than 800 salted pigs for transport to Shanghai. The ship departed from Qingkou, but when it sailed on the Qingkou sea, it suddenly encountered two pirate ships, with a large group of bandits driving them up and ordering the boat to stop. When the crew saw this, they wanted to turn the rudder and sail back to avoid danger, but they were spotted by the pirates, who opened fire on the Golden Ship. Two dockworkers and crew members were wounded by the bullets, and there were also more than a dozen holes in the bow. At this point, all the crew members were panic-stricken and had to run and hide in the cabin. At this time, two pirate ships had quickly sailed over, surrounded the boat from the left and right, and swarmed onto the ship, driving the people on board to the stern and watching them with guns. The pirates searched everywhere and found only a little more than two hundred dollars in a small leather suitcase, as well as more than ten account books, and cargo invoices and donation tickets from the merchants. The pirates were very angry that such a large ship only had such a small amount of money, and threw the leather suitcase and account books into the sea. Then they searched the crew's beds and took all the silver dollars they could find. Still not satisfied, they opened the cargo hold and forced the crew to start loading the salted pigs and move them to the pirate ships. When two crew members refused to move the goods, they were beaten in the face until they bled. All the salted pigs in the middle cabin were moved and stolen. As the pirate ships were leaving, they dragged two helmsmen to the pirate ships, intending to kidnap them and take them away. The two men begged on the ground, and were finally released. The two pirate ships then sailed east. The Gold Ship is now sailing to Liuhe to dock, and the injured crew members have been sent to the hospital, where one of the crew members is in critical condition. Yesterday, the shipowner came to Shanghai to report the information to the newspaper and various cargo numbers, but the ship needs to be repaired before it can sail, and the losses are very heavy.

Robbery, Theft, and Gunshot Wounding 140

▲Laundry Maid Injured

The Baohua Laundry, located at No. 20 Pishou Nalu in the French Concession, is owned by Zhou Abaob, a native of Ningbo. Yesterday at 11:30 PM, three robbers, all armed with handguns, arrived and threatened the owner, ransacking the place at will. However, the laundry had no valuables, only a dozen sets of customers' laundry, none of which were of much value. Frustrated, they demanded money from Zhou's wife, Liu, who replied that she had none. Enraged, the robbers fired a shot, hitting Liu in the right foot. The bullet exited, causing profuse bleeding. The gang fled in a panic. Police officers No. 356 from the Songshan Road police station arrived and took Liu to Renji Hospital. After treatment by the doctor, the police took her back to the police station to report the incident and investigate the suspects.

Account Collector of Ning-Shao Steamer Robbed 141

▲Over One Hundred Yuan Stolen on Avenue Edward VII

When the Xin Ning-Shao steamer of the Ning-Shao Company departs from Shanghai, the company sends a ticket seller to the ship. Each day, the ticket revenue is delivered to the company's accounting department after the ship departs. On the afternoon of the 14th of this month at 5:30 PM, after the Xin Ning-Shao steamer left port, more than one thousand yuan in ticket revenue, collected by staff member Xie Jinsheng, was divided into two leather bags. One bag contained over nine hundred yuan, and the other contained 184.8 yuan. Xie hired a rickshaw to go from the South City to Jiangxi Road. One bag was placed under him, concealed by his long coat, while the other bag was placed at his feet. When they arrived in front of the International Savings Society on Avenue Edward VII, two men suddenly appeared, brandishing handguns and warning Xie not to make a sound. One robber snatched a bag and fled. Fortunately, the stolen bag contained only the smaller sum of 180+ yuan; the bag with over nine hundred yuan was not taken. The company reported the incident to the police yesterday for investigation.

Police Request Withdrawal of Lawsuit Against Wang the Monk 142

▲Other Than the Same Name ▲Cannot Prove He Was a Kidnapper

Chen Qiwu, the son of Chen Bingqian, a comprador at Jardine Matheson, was kidnapped on April 4th last year. The kidnappers demanded a ransom of 100,000 yuan. He later escaped after one of the kidnappers went to check the ransom note and let him go. The police successively arrested several kidnappers, who were tried and convicted by the court. However, after being arrested, the kidnappers confessed that the handguns they used were supplied by Wang the Monk. The court issued an arrest warrant and ordered the police to arrest him and bring him to justice. A year has passed, and recently, the Huishi police station arrested Wang the Monk, a native of Ningbo, and sent him to the Special District Court. However, Wang the Monk absolutely denied any involvement in the kidnapping. The court then presented the case to the imprisoned kidnappers for verification, but they claimed that the handguns were handed over by A Feng, A Rong, and others. The judge ordered Wang to be detained pending the arrival of witnesses for further questioning. The police investigation revealed that A Rong and others had previously lived on Youheng Road, but fled without a trace at the end of last year due to unpaid rent. Furthermore, there was no evidence to prove that Wang the Monk was indeed a kidnapper. Yesterday morning, Wang was escorted to the Special Court, where the investigation results were reported. The police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, stated that besides the defendant's name being the same as the wanted kidnapper, there was no other evidence against him. It is now proposed to withdraw the lawsuit. Judge Wu ordered that the case, which had been tried several times, be opened for debate immediately, and the verdict would be announced later. After the lawyers on both sides debated, the court ordered Wang the Monk to be detained pending sentencing on the morning of the 19th.

▲Suspected Arson by Petty Thief

Yesterday morning around 2:00 AM, a fire broke out in a row of fifteen sheds behind the Dong family's residence in Hongzhen. According to the owner, who reported the incident to the No. 3 Precinct of the No. 5 District Public Security Bureau, the fire was caused by arson. The sheds were next to a dyeing shop. Three weeks ago, a petty thief tried to steal cloth and was recognized by Yang, holding a grudge and setting the fire.

Ruixiang Electrical Supplies and Others Penalized for Not Affixing Revenue Stamps 144

▲Repeat Offender Fined Double, Forty Yuan

Last Tuesday, seven businesses, including Tianfu Southern Goods Store, were fined for not affixing revenue stamps to their invoices. The remaining three businesses, including Ruixiang Electrical Supplies, did not appear in court and their hearings were rescheduled for Saturday, as previously reported. It is now reported that yesterday (the 15th), the Special District Court summoned the three businesses, including Ruixiang, and Judge Tao Dejun convened a hearing. Ruixiang Electrical Supplies, being a repeat offender, was fined double, forty yuan, for intentionally evading the affixing of revenue stamps. The other two businesses, Xiuse Restaurant and Shenhe Tin Foil Shop, were each fined thirty yuan.

Record of the Opening of the Nanshi Rice Wharf 152

The Nanshi Bean and Rice Industry Wharf officially opened on the 15th. Most rice boats went there continuously, with the exception of a small number of rice boats that still believed gossip and observed, because of the convenience of loading and unloading and the comfort of berthing, It is said that the wharf fees imposed on rice boats were recognized and paid by both merchants and customers, so that the boat owners had no monetary loss. As soon as Mr. Zhu Zixiang makes the matter clear and explains this misunderstanding, it will not be difficult for those who were previously waiting to happily follow. At the same time, all rice stores in Nanshi were opened at the Fengji Wharf, which has now become a center of rice markets. The amount of goods available and the sales numbers can be known at a glance, and the market conditions are also uniform, without the drawbacks of rising in some places and falling in others. It eliminates not a few difficulties for merchants and customers.

Bursting of the French Concession Water Pipe 153

▲Turned Into a Watery Land ▲Already Repaired

Yesterday morning around 6:30 AM, in front of the South Railway Station, at the intersection of Chenjiaqiao Hongmao Lane, south of the Huashang Electrical Company, a water pipe belonging to the French Concession Water Company burst. In an instant, water gushed out into the streets, rising to six or seven inches, turning the area into a watery land and blocking traffic. A small number of trolleys from the Huashang Tram Company had already left the factory and started running, while other vehicles which hadn't yet left the factory, were stopped due to being blocked by the water. The resulting delay lasted for two hours, until 8:30 AM, when they were finally able to leave the factory and resume operation. Upon learning of the incident, the water company immediately sent Chinese and Western employees to carry out repairs, which were completed by 5:00 PM in the afternoon.

Winter Relief in Beiping 154

Mr. Zhou Jingfu, the director of the China Relief Society's office in Beiping, and Mr. She Guisheng, the director of the office in Tianjin, have repeatedly telegraphed appeals for the disaster victims in Beiping, requesting that winter relief be organized to save the people from the disaster. The Society has transported 6,000 cotton-padded clothes to Tianjin and has entrusted Mr. Zhou and Mr. She to purchase 2,000 sets in Tianjin for distribution. In addition, the Society continues to operate a porridge factory outside Chaoyangmen. With the provincial government moving to Tianjin this year, the city's economic situation has become increasingly bleak, and the number of people waiting for food has increased several times. Although the Society has repeatedly received letters and telegrams from Mr. Zhou and others requesting assistance, it has had to try its best to maintain the Chaoyangmen porridge factory, even with its limited relief funds. In addition to continuing to have Mrs. Bao oversee the operation, two more factories will be established.

Weather Report 158

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: "The weather is changing, there is rain on the Shandong coast, and a low-pressure system is moving towards the northeast-east, passing over Korea, so there will be a cyclone there. There will be strong southwest winds to northwest winds on the Shandong and local coasts. South of Madang Island, the winds will be non-directional, with occasional fog in some areas." Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in Shanghai was 71.6 degrees, and the lowest was 46.2 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 56.7 degrees, and the lowest was 51.6 degrees.

To the Editor, In the "Union News" column on the 14th, Proposal No. 1 in the 15th joint meeting minutes of our union reported that management's Wu Axiang hadn't fully paid Yao Xinzhu's cabin pay. Our union sent an investigator to verify, and it was confirmed that Wu Axiang had already fully paid the workers' wages. The previous case was a misunderstanding. This matter concerns the welfare of labor and management, and we ask your newspaper to publish this in the "Letters" column for correction. Thank you for your service. Sincerely, Shanghai Sand and Gravel Barging Union, November 15th.

To the Editor, After reading the article "Disputes in the Silk Factory Opening" in your newspaper, the description of Chen Zhongxiang's disruptions seems inaccurate. On the 14th, our union received a letter from the Yuanfeng branch requesting guidance for a temporary meeting of the branch. Our union appointed Chen Zhongxiang as the representative. However, the factory manager, Zhu Jing'an, disagreed with Chen's tone and pulled out a gun, ordering him not to speak. He also telegraphed the police station, and the police arrested Chen. All the employees of the factory witnessed this. They reported to the union in this way. Therefore, we request that you accurately report the details of this situation so that justice may be served. Sincerely, Shanghai Silk Factory Workers Union, East District Silk Factory, November 15th.

To the Editor, Please note that the "Road Construction Levy Regulations" have been published in various newspapers, but there is an error in Article 17. We are making the following corrections: "Article 17: If the tax is overdue for more than three years and is still not paid, the competent bureau of the municipal government may notify the landowner in writing 30 days in advance of a scheduled auction of all or part of the fixed property on the land to the extent necessary to offset the amount owed. Any remaining funds will be returned to the original delinquent taxpayer." We hope your newspaper will publish this correction. Sincerely, Shanghai Municipal Government Fifth Section.

Jiangsu Education Fee Management Office Rectifies Tax Revenue 160

▲Liyang and Jiangning Finance Bureau Chiefs Neglect Duties and Embezzle Funds ▲A Letter Requesting the Provincial Government to Punish

A letter from the Jiangsu Education Fee Management Office to the Provincial Government stated: "We are writing to inform you that the current educational funding situation in this province is extremely difficult. We have repeatedly ordered that the divided-up Mang Cao and Ya taxes from each county be used exclusively for educational purposes and not be diverted in the slightest. However, Pan Bin, the former director of the Liyang Finance Bureau, had a total outstanding balance of 27,924.285 yuan in silver from the collected and over-collected Mang Cao and Ya taxes as of August. Despite repeated reminders, he has not remitted the funds. For the September designated allocation of 1,486.88 yuan in silver, the director underreported the amount and falsely claimed that it was deposited in another account, failing to comply with the regulations. Gu Dingming, the resident supervisor, has reported the facts in detail. It is clear that the director is under arrest in the province for another case of corruption. If these outstanding educational funds are not thoroughly investigated and pursued, how can we deter others and ensure protection? In addition to sending separate letters, we are hereby requesting that Your Excellency investigate and instruct the Finance Department to handle this case together, imposing strict punishment and ordering the full payment of the outstanding special provincial education funds to protect public funds, without any leniency. Your public service will be greatly appreciated. Please reply to this letter. Jiangsu Provincial Government, Niu Yongjian."

Another letter to the Provincial Government stated: "We are writing to inform you that Huang Shoushan, the director of the Jiangning County Finance Bureau, has not paid attention to the allocation of funds from the land tax for provincial educational expenses since taking office. The former Cao rice and provincial taxes were special funds for education, but he did not remit a single cent. After the implementation of the new regulations, he arbitrarily shelved the orders and instructions from the departments and commissions, without reporting them. After repeated urgent telegrams, he began to report the collected amounts intermittently. As of August, the figures were checked and found to be discrepant and erroneous, and he also failed to report the amount collected from the first season of the year. It was only after our office instructed him to investigate in detail that he supplemented the report. According to the report from Supervisor Fang Jie, the names of the items delivered to the county granary have never been clear. Although we ordered a thorough investigation, we did not receive a clear reply, which, combined with the failure to report the amount of Cao rice collected, raises suspicions. Educational funding is urgently needed and has reached a critical point. The reported collection of special funds is overdue and has not been remitted despite repeated reminders. Such negligence of duty is inexcusable and has caused delays. He should be punished according to the law to maintain the essential needs. We are hereby requesting that Your Excellency investigate, and we earnestly hope that you will be mindful of the extreme difficulty of educational funding, provide strong support and protection, and promptly refer Director Huang Shoushan for disciplinary action and impose punishment to deter others. At the same time, please order a serious rectification in accordance with the regulations, and monthly clear remittances. The future of education is at stake. In addition to sending a letter to the Finance Department, we are writing to Jiangsu Provincial Government, Niu Yongjian."

Eighth District Party Headquarters' Second Public Telegram Regarding the Chung Kung School Disturbance 162

(Kuomintang News Agency) The Eighth District Party Headquarters of this city issued a second public telegram regarding the Chung Kung School disturbance, which reads as follows: Urgent, please forward this from Shanghai newspaper offices to all levels of Party Headquarters, organizations, groups, and schools nationwide for their attention. Ma Junwu, the former president of Wusong China Public School, shielded reactionaries and suppressed Party members. Our headquarters has listed the facts and issued the first public telegram on October 25th. It received responses from Party Headquarters in various locations. Knowing that he could not withstand public anger, Ma Junwu used a pretext to leave the school and resigned from the school board. The school board approved the resignation and appointed Yu Youren as his successor. Considering that Mr. Yu is a Central Committee member of our Party, a founder of the school with the longest history and closest ties, our headquarters issued a telegram on the 9th of this month to welcome him. However, the reactionary elements in the school have become even more rampant, forming illegal delegations, establishing armed pickets, coercing student will, and using the name of the whole body to express their oath to support Ma Junwu and forcefully reject Mr. Yu Youren's arrival. They tore down the banners of welcome to Mr. Yu from the First Branch of the Eighth District and the students of the school, violently beat Wang Guoping, a standing committee member of the First Branch of the Eighth District, and students Long Yingjie and Li Fanchou, and forcibly locked down the auditorium and classrooms, forcing students to boycott classes. Such illegal acts are extremely reactionary. Upon careful investigation, the reason why the reactionary elements in the school dare to act so rampantly is due to a few teachers in the school acting as accomplices. When Hu Shih was the principal of the school, he cultivated reactionary forces among the students for his own use and founded the New Moon magazine to publish reactionary opinions, which eventually led to his dismissal from society. Still ambitious, he strongly recommended Ma Junwu, whose political views were the same as his, as the principal. Since Ma Junwu arrived at the school, his various violations of the Party were not only following the old ways, but also intensified, leading to the increasingly rampant reactionary atmosphere. After Ma Junwu's departure, Hu Shih was greatly angered upon hearing the news after returning to Shanghai from the north, where he was unaware of the events. He immediately incited the reactionary students he had long nurtured to launch a movement to support Ma. Hu believes that with Ma gone and Yu coming, the reactionary forces he has painstakingly cultivated over the years will be wiped out, so he has no choice but to make a final struggle. On the 12th of this month, he dared to personally take over the duties of the chairman of the student union and incite students to expand the unrest. Hu Shih also told people that he did not cherish Mr. Ma, but because he had always opposed Kuomintang members coming to lead Chung Kung, he had to carry out his claim this time. Hu Shih is a down-and-out villain and a bored politician. Although he has been severely warned by the Central Government, he still does not know how to restrain himself. If he is not given due punishment, how can he deter reactionaries and prevent others from following suit. Furthermore, it has been found that Luo Longji, the head of the Department of Political Economy of the school, is an important member of the Statist faction. He and Zhang Yaoxian, the person in charge of the faction in Chung Kung, have been arrested by the Municipal Public Security Bureau. Later, Luo was bailed out by a powerful person and escaped the law. However, Luo still dares to hide near the school and direct various activities of the reactionaries. He should also be severely punished to punish the ringleaders. Furthermore, it has been found that Wang Hongshi, the chief of general affairs of the school, is Ma's personal friend and has been working very hard for this disturbance. All the actions of the delegation are presided over by Wang Hongshi. He personally attends and guides every meeting, uses school administration as protection for his rule, misappropriates student union fees for economic assistance, and personally hands over the keys to the delegation to lock down the classrooms and force students to boycott classes. We request the higher Party headquarters to severely punish all these reactionary leaders and reactionary elements in the school. Our headquarters, witnessing the chaos, cannot bear to sit idly by. In addition to submitting a request to the higher Party headquarters to severely punish the reactionary leaders and reactionary elements of the school, we also hope that all sectors will share the same hatred and jointly condemn them. We are infinitely hopeful and pray. This is our public telegram. Respectfully, the Executive Committee of the Eighth District of the Shanghai Special Municipality of the Chinese Kuomintang, bowing respectfully.

Reply Letter from Li Liangong, Head of the Department and Professor of the Agricultural College of Labor University (Continued) 165

That Mr. Chen is opposed by the students of the Horticulture Department certainly has a complicated background. Otherwise, it would not have erupted so suddenly at this time. The coincidence is as such. As for the reason why the students of the Chemistry Department oppose Mr. Fang and Mr. Wu, it is because Mr. Chen made public to the students his private letters disagreeing with Mr. Tie Ming's coming to the school. The invitation of Mr. Tie is another matter. Mr. Chen has repeatedly expressed the same opposition to Mr. Fang and Mr. Wu. However, Mr. Chen is very scheming and has been plotting to harm his colleagues for more than a day. He used a lightning-fast method to publish private letters from a month ago at this time. Mr. Chen's maliciousness is truly questionable. From that day on, Mr. Fang, Mr. Wu, and Mr. Chen could not come to the school. And the magic tricks performed by Mr. Chen became more and more bizarre. In addition to openly spreading rumors to the students, such as "Greater Hunanism" and "Fang and Wu are giving up the deanship of the College of Science," there were also detectives and spies all over the college. Every move of the colleagues was monitored. The solemn and splendid university became a ghost realm of miasma and black smoke. Colleagues have been forced to be unable to exercise their professorial duties for three weeks now. Mr. Chen initially glossed over the situation, saying that the professors' suspension of classes was a leave of absence and that the news in the newspapers was a rumor created by the secretariat. Then, he adopted a strategy of breaking them down one by one, entrusting someone to mediate with Mr. Chen Guorong, but Fang and Wu believed that they had to leave. Mr. Fang's class has asked Mr. Jiang to replace him, and Mr. Wu's class has asked Mr. Tie to replace him. For the education community to have this kind of behavior cannot but be said to be a major stain on Mr. Chen's character. The above is about the content and process of the students' opposition to Mr. Chen, Mr. Fang, and Mr. Wu. (2) The letter states that the letter from colleagues to the students of the Agricultural College is full of slanders, but Mr. Chen did not list the facts or argue the key points of the slanders. For example, regarding the item of Principal Tie Ying, when the Ministry of Education issued an order last year to recruit students, the issue of the president of Labor University was not shaken. Mr. Chen said that the colleagues of Labor University unanimously wanted him to take the position of president and had entrusted someone to telegraph Chairman Chiang, but that person did not allow it. Mr. Chen also said that the colleagues planned to ask a certain mayor to serve as the president and that he himself would serve as the vice president and still ask that person to introduce him and introduce Mr. Chen to talk. Later, that person talked to that mayor about the Labor University issue and said that Mr. Wu Zhihui had come forward to mediate and that there was no shakeup in the matter of changing the president. Only then did that person realize that Mr. Chen's request was completely fabricated and laughed silently. Not long after, Mr. Chen wanted to support a certain gentleman as president and himself as vice president. All the colleagues of Labor University knew about it, and there should be more than hundreds of people who can prove it. (The names of a certain person, a certain mayor, and a certain gentleman are temporarily hidden because they involve too many people. If necessary, they can all testify.) Are these true facts also said by Mr. Chen to be rumors? At a time when the entire school unanimously did not accept the strange punishment of the Ministry of Education, Mr. Chen uniquely had a different heart and secretly campaigned to overthrow the highest administrative head of the school, with himself as the president or vice president. Is this not a conspiracy for power and harm to the school? As for the words of colluding with the Ministry of Education, it is a statement by the gentleman himself. The Ministry of Education is the highest educational administrative organ. How can there be "collusion"? Can Mr. Chen also point out where the basis for this kind of rumor comes from? Since Mr. Chen denies the organization of the school protection group, can Mr. Chen also point out the evidence that this kind of leaflet was fabricated by the opposition party? The smoke incident occurred at your residence on October 31. It was not until November 2 that some colleagues learned from Zhang's aunt that Mr. Chen said it was a frame-up and false accusation by colleagues. Then, the smoke incident that Mr. Chen committed when he served as a standing committee member and secretary of the preparatory committee of the 46th Army Special Party Department in August 1928, was also falsely accused by whom? And since there is a neighborhood number that can be pointed out, the name of the accuser can be easily inquired. The Public Security Bureau is a government agency and certainly will not make groundless claims. It is hoped that Mr. Chen will clearly answer this matter. As for Mr. Chen's sending anonymous threatening letters, saying that they were done by colleagues to falsely accuse colleagues, this is truly wishful thinking. Mr. Chen is truly smart! You must know that the opposition of colleagues to Mr. Chen is in a clear attitude and a proper method. On the one hand, we must take into account the dignity of the promotion of education. At the same time, we must maintain the personality of university professors. How can we follow Mr. Chen's example, use all base means to exclude dissidents. As for who is framing, falsely accusing, and anonymously threatening, since the Public Security Bureau has a case to investigate, Mr. Chen must clearly point it out to dispel doubts. Li Huitang and Jiang Daozhang Win Hard Court Doubles Championship 169

▲Yesterday, they lost to Shi Guiya and Bode 3-2.

▲Today, Jiang Daozhang will decide the singles match against Taoshi.

The final of the French Chamber of Commerce's men's doubles championship on hard court tennis was held at 2:00 PM yesterday between the team of Li Huitang and Jiang Daozhang and the team of Shi Guiya and Bode. The two sides were evenly matched and difficult to distinguish. Therefore, the situation was quite tense. After five fierce sets, the winner was finally decided. As a result, the Jiang and Li team won the championship, defeating the Shi and Bu team with scores of 4-6, 6-4, 7-5, 3-6, and 6-4. The situation is described below:

▲In the first set, Shi and Bu won the first two games, and Jiang and Li won one game, then it became 3-1. Jiang and Li carefully fought back. After a long battle in the next game, Jiang and Li won back one game. After winning this game, Jiang and Li's momentum suddenly increased, adding two more games and taking the lead. It looked very easy, but Shi and Bu were not to be outdone, working hard to take three consecutive games, winning Jiang and Li with 6-4.

▲In the second set, Jiang and Li initially led 3-1, which looked very smooth, but the next three games were lost in succession, falling behind 3-4. Jiang and Li cautiously made their moves, often using high balls to return from the rear. When there was an opportunity, they would launch a strong attack. As expected, they succeeded, winning three consecutive games as they wished, also winning 6-4.

▲The situation in the third set was very tense, with each side following each other closely, without letting up. It was also the highlight, with each side giving a good performance. But Shi and Bu took the lead, and Jiang and Li followed closely behind. After 5-5, Jiang and Li jumped ahead, finishing in one go, winning two consecutive games, winning 7-5, and becoming a score of 2-1, with Jiang and Li taking the lead.

▲Jiang and Li were often in a dangerous situation in the fourth set and did not improve. After the score was 4-2 (Shi and Bu winning), Jiang and Li suddenly made a clever move, winning a lot of cheers. But the seventh game was still lost, which was a pity. Instead, the situation became more dangerous. It was impossible to turn the tide. Shi and Bu won with 6-3, making the score 2-2.

▲The key to the fifth set was in this final set. The two sides continued their efforts to fight to the death. Jiang and Li's close coordination and steady combat repeatedly took the upper hand. Although Shi and Bu tried hard to chase to 3-3, Jiang and Li won three consecutive games in the following games, winning again with 6-4, and winning the championship. Together with Lin and Qiu's winning the grass court doubles championship the day before, it added a lot of glory to the Chinese tennis world.

Also, at 2:00 PM today, Jiang Daozhang will play against Taoshi to decide the hard court singles tennis championship.

A Chuckle 185

— Hai Ke

▲Gentleman (to a woman leading a child): "Madam, your child is so tall. How old is he this year?"

Woman: "He's ten this year."

Gentleman: "What good fortune! I'd say you yourself aren't even thirty."

Woman (somewhat unnaturally): "I've forgotten what year I was born in."

Gentleman: "Then what century were you born in? Surely you remember that."

▲Robber (jumping out of the darkness, blocking a young man's path): "Friend, be smart! Hand over your money, or I'll smash your head!"

Young Man: "Go ahead. Living in Shanghai, all mixed up, one doesn't really need a brain. But money is indispensable."

Police Officer: "Now that you've saved this person from drowning, what will become of him?"

Savior: "I was just about to leave when he hanged himself from a tree."

Police Officer: "Then why didn't you save him again?"

Savior: "I thought he was hanging his clothes on the tree to dry because they got wet."

▲A: "I fell for her at first sight."

B: "Then why don't you propose to her?"

A: "But then I saw her a few more times."

Trivial Records of the Anniversary of the Premier's Birth 186

— Sun Choucheng

The twelfth of the month was the sixty-fifth anniversary of the birth of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, Premier of the Chinese Nationalist Party. Various circles in this city held a commemorative meeting at the Republican Cinema on Minguo Road in the South City. The general situation has already been recorded in this newspaper. The following is a supplementary record of the trivial matters seen and heard on that day.

At the entrance of the meeting place, a white cloth banner with red characters was hung high, which read: "Shanghai Circles Celebrate the Sixty-Fifth Anniversary of the Birth of Premier Sun Yat-sen." The national flags were arranged in a crossed shape. I went before nine o'clock. The entrance was already crowded with viewers. Upon entering, I received a copy of the Premier's Birthday Commemorative Special Edition published by the Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Municipal Executive Committee and the Sixth Branch of the Third District. One section contains the works of Yang Qingyuan and others, comparing the birth of the Premier to a global alarm bell, saying that the sound of the bell affected not only one corner of China, or one place in East Asia, but the entire world. In addition to the texts of Wang Xiaolai and others, the other section also contained a photo of the Premier's childhood study place, titled "Cuiheng Temple School and Its Vicinity". There was a large tree in the photo, with curved branches, which was quite artistic. On that day, because there were so many guests who arrived, all the seats were occupied, so the meeting started on time. They were singing the Party song. Chairman Yang Qingyuan, wearing a blue silk robe, stated the purpose of the meeting, in addition to describing the Premier's birth in Cuiheng Village, Xiangshan County, Guangdong Province, he also raised two points in his life's work. (1) He invented the Three Principles of the People to save the dying China. (2) The revolutionary spirit was like a day for forty years, never giving up and fighting to the end. He hoped that those attending the meeting would continue the Premier's great spirit, follow the Three Principles of the People, and complete the Premier's legacy. While he was reporting, suddenly a person, about thirty years old, wearing a Zhongshan suit, holding several books, pushed through the crowd to the stage and bowed three times. The audience was puzzled. They later learned that he was late due to something, and he had not participated in the ceremony when the meeting started, so he made a special trip to pay his respects, which showed the depth of his belief in the Premier. Wu Bokang, a representative of the Municipal Party Department, also wore a blue robe. During his speech, he said that the Premier had a healthy spirit, so he was able to not be afraid of difficulties and fight with the environment. He hoped that all comrades would exercise their bodies and work hard. Chen Kecheng, a representative of the municipal government, wore a suit. He was very polite in his speech, saying that he had not prepared a speech for today's grand event, and he did not dare to disobey the chairman's order. He reported his scattered opinions to you, not a speech to you. Divided into three points (1) Cultivate personality. (2) Enrich intelligence. (3) Work hard on construction. A detailed explanation was given. Then Xu Ji, a representative of the Overseas Chinese Coordination Association, gave a speech. He described in detail that more than 30 years ago, when he was in Taiwan, he talked about the revolutionary process when he first met with the Premier. All the representatives present on that day were under the age of 30. What Xu Jun said was about things before they were born. It was as if the students in the school were listening to stories. They all listened attentively with great interest. The one who followed Xu Jun's speech was a certain overseas Chinese who had been forced to return to China by the Dutch government. He described in detail the various forms of abuse by the Dutch imperialism in collecting entry taxes from overseas Chinese, expelling Chinese teachers back to the country, opposing the Kuomintang, prohibiting the reading of the Three Principles of the People, and not allowing memorial weeks to be held, as well as closing the border for a long time during entry, and using body examinations as an excuse. He was even moved to tears. The entire audience had angry eyes and gritted teeth to express their indignation. A proposal was put forward on the spot to strongly protest to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs against the unreasonable oppression of our overseas Chinese by the Dutch government in the Nanyang region. The Sino-Dutch treaty has expired, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs should be asked to immediately announce its abolition. When this proposal was passed, not only did everyone raise their hands unanimously, but they also shouted "Pass, pass!" A kind of passionate state was unprecedented in the meeting. It is enough to show that the people's hearts are not dead, and the country still has a future. I am returning and recording this to never forget.

Worthy of Praise for Not Pocketing Money Found 187

— Mei

Ms. Shi Xi'en, head nurse of the Nanjing medical community, found 100 yuan in cash on Friday evening (November 7) in Jiaozhuangyuan Alley. On Tuesday (this month, 11th), she discovered that it had been left by Hang Hai, a specialist of the Ministry of Railways, and was official funds in his possession. After the owner stated the location of the loss, it was confirmed to be correct, and Hu Xuanming, director of the Health Department of the Ministry of Railways, issued a certificate. Li Handuo, a pastor of the Methodist Church, also issued a guarantee. Ms. Shi returned the money without taking any of it. This matter is worthy of being praised by the world, and it is especially rare for it to come from a woman. Therefore, it is recorded. (Rejecting a reward)

Examination of Male to Female Transformation 188

— Xiu Jun

I read in the newspaper of the 29th of last month about a 21-year-old man who suddenly transformed into a woman. I was surprised to no end. Who is this man? It is Shen Tianfang of Zhuji. Since the age of sixteen, he had abdominal pain and bloody stools every month. Doctors diagnosed him with venereal disease. Only Wang Jiren diagnosed him as a female pseudohermaphrodite. After performing a dissection and artificial vaginoplasty, he actually transformed into a woman. Alas, this is truly a strange story. I have always loved to be curious and have tried my best to collect information about strange events for reference. The details of this male-to-female transformation, including the surname, name, and origin, are clear and distinct. It cannot be compared to rumors that are passed down from the neighborhood and have no basis. Therefore, I have listed the following similar cases recorded in ancient books.

The Book of Han, Five Elements Records, says: "During the Jianping era, there was a man in Yuzhang who turned into a woman, married someone, and gave birth to a son." The Book of Later Han, Five Elements Records, says: "In the seventh year of Jian'an, there was a man in Yuejun who turned into a woman." At that time, Zhou Qun reported, "There was also this anomaly during the reign of Emperor Ai." Jiangnan History says: "During the time of the Later Lord of the Southern Tang Dynasty, Ouyang Zi of Luling was about to marry a woman when he suddenly turned into a woman. Later, she married and had children." The History of Ming, Five Elements Records, says: "In December of the second year of Longqing, Li Liangyu, a man from Jinglu, turned into a woman." The Outline of Love Stories says: "Two merchants in Luoyang were best friends. Suddenly, one of the younger ones had unbearable abdominal pain. His friend treated him, and fortunately, he did not die. After more than ten days, he transformed into a woman. The matter was reported to the officials. They reported it to the court. The two merchants were both unmarried, so they were ordered to be married as husband and wife. This happened in the Bingxu year of the Wanli era." The Nanyang Prefecture Records says: "In the third year of Tianqi, there was a man from Tang County who turned into a woman."

The above six items all clearly indicate the source, which is different from those who do not believe without evidence. However, the Jiangnan History records that Ouyang Zi of Luling transformed into a woman, which is slightly different from the one recorded in the Spring and Autumn of the Ten Kingdoms, which was Zeng. The History of Ming says that Li Liangyu's incident was in December of the second year of Longqing, while the Second Shen Manuscript says it was in May of the Wuchen year. The Compendium of Materia Medica also says that Li Liangyu had abdominal pain from time to time in January of the first year of Longqing, and the pain did not stop on February 9 of the second year. By April, the testicles had unknowingly shrunk into the abdomen and transformed into a woman's vagina. Menstruation also began the following month, and she began to change into women's clothing. The same Li incident, the month is not only two ways, why? I secretly think that these kinds of textual research are only for humor and strangeness, and have nothing to do with the main purpose. According to the example of writing, it is enough to have two theories coexisting.

A Few Words on Stomach Problems 189

— Ma Yinliang

After the publication of my book "General Ideas on Stomach Problems", I was honored by the people of the country. The first edition of 3,000 copies had been sold out by more than half in less than ten days. From this, it can be seen that there are many people in the country who suffer from stomach problems, and their desire to seek treatment is sincere. How should doctors carefully study, understand the condition, and treat it?

According to reports from doctors in hospitals across the country, people with stomach problems are mostly from the intellectual class. Generally, those in the education, banking, and newspaper industries are most prone to stomach problems. This is due to the lack of exercise and excessive mental labor without rest. Therefore, the daily work and rest should be on time, and a certain amount of daily exercise is essential. Even a slight walk is enough to recuperate the spirit and boost physical strength. In the past, the great German philosopher Kant always took a walk once a day and enjoyed a high age. This is his proof.

When stomach problems first occur, you only need to eat less and rest quietly, and you can recover on your own without taking medicine. This is the principle of natural treatment. If you pay attention to your diet on the one hand and use medicine on the other, the disease will be easier to cure. Otherwise, if you only rely on the power of medicine without paying attention to your diet, it will not be easy to cure. If you are unfortunate enough to turn into a chronic disease, then treatment will be even more difficult.

Journalists are prone to stomach problems. This is because their duties mean that they cannot have a fixed place to eat and live. Busy banquets are also a major cause. After banquets, sitting at a desk and holding a pen is most harmful to the stomach. Therefore, journalists should rest a little after banquets, and it is better to eat less. And the host of the banquet should also treat reporters differently and never force them to eat. You must know that forcing people to eat more is to promote their illness.

After the treatment of stomach problems, the appetite will inevitably increase greatly. At this time, you should pay special attention to the hygiene of your diet. You should also strictly avoid small snacks. This is a natural phenomenon during recovery. Those who suffer from stomach problems must be careful.

The hygiene of the stomach and the methods of preventing stomach diseases, in thousands of words, are nothing more than two fixed words, namely, a fixed time and a fixed amount of food. Stomach problems are mostly caused by eating too much and being too full. Therefore, if you can follow this rule before you get sick, your stomach will not get sick. If you can follow this rule after you get sick, the disease will be easier to cure.

(Attached announcement: There are not many books left in the General Ideas on Stomach Problems. Please send a letter to my clinic at No. 589, Datong Road, Baik Road to request it. Please do so as soon as possible, or you may be too late.

Travel Notes of Southeast Asia (73) 190

There are still many places along the Burma-Yunnan border that grow poppies, so opium is produced here and sold to various countries. This item is difficult to prohibit. The price is too high. Everyone loves profit. The area where there are big profits, you cannot suppress them. Also, starting from Yunnan, there is no strict inspection of mountainous areas of various countries. Therefore, private exchanges and land routes have never been free. Also, there is no need for a passport. It is very difficult to prohibit it. Chinese people in Northern Burma, whether they are laborers or not, have a smoky complexion at a glance. It is also pitiful. As a result, another kind of superstition has been added, saying that those who work in mines cannot avoid miasma if they do not eat opium. I said, this must be a smoking rumor. Or superstition. In the past, many local bandits died in my hometown. Some people hated them and ate their hearts. As a result, the custom of eating human hearts has been formed. And they superstitiously believe that it can cure diseases. Each one costs four thousand five hundred. It is also a kind of superstition. What is even more ridiculous is that when I left Shaoguan fifteen or sixteen years ago, I went from Shaoguan to Nanxiong, and from Nanxiong to Dagan in Jiangxi. The sedan chair carriers had to eat opium. They were as black and thin as ghosts. I felt sorry for them and asked them, "Why do you eat opium?" Their answer was unbelievable. They said, "How can we carry the sedan chair if we don't eat opium?" I laughed heartily and could not explain it to them. They never understood that carrying the sedan chair was the result of eating opium. Instead, they mistook the cause for the effect, thinking that they could not carry the sedan chair without eating opium. Ridiculous things in the world are often like this. Now, people in Northern Burma are creating this kind of rumor, which is similar.

On the eighth, there was a Namtu train to Nabiao. I got on the train. The price was two shields. The price of the open-top car was half a shield. I met some Indians in the car and asked about Gandhi. They replied that he had been sent to the Bombay Prison by the British. I asked what we should call Gandhi. Can we call him Mr.? They replied that we Indians all call him Mahatma. That is, the meaning of the great hero. I asked, "Do you believe that Mahatma Gandhi can save you and get freedom?" They said, "Yes." I asked, "Does Gandhi believe in Islam?" They said, "No." I asked, "Is it Buddhism?" They said, "Close to it. But it is Hinduism." I said, "I always have a big doubt. Why do we in the East all believe in Buddhism, but your country does not believe in it and believes in Hinduism? What is the reason?" They replied, "Each has its advantages." I asked, "Do you believe in Gandhi more than our Sun Yat-sen?" They replied, "Sun Yat-sen is far inferior to Gandhi." I said, "Gandhi is lofty in philosophy and religion, while Sun Yat-sen is great in revolutionary work. Also, our revolution has now been 70 to 80% successful, while India is still early." They replied, "We don't have weapons." I said, "Indeed. We still need to work hard."

Warmth in the Heart (316) 191

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 15: Shedding Tears on All Sides, Sadness in Red Love, Wholeheartedness in Low Green Intent

Lin Fanzi said, "That's strange. Mr. Long has always asked for a play, but he doesn't take a promiscuous attitude. He can be called a loyal customer. Why did he also jump ship?" Long Ziyun said, "There is no ship jumping. This Green Intent is also a member of the Bao family. Yesterday, I had already asked for Bao Meiyun's concert. I knew that she had caught a cold recently. She had a fever and couldn't come out. A little girl came in her place. That little girl has another sign. Her name is Green Intent. They also took her down. Her face is not bad. She is also very quiet. Anyway, A-su always follows. Writing Meiyun, writing Green Intent, is the same in the end." It turned out that the Bao family in Puqing Lane was called the Bao Family Five Clouds. They have Bao Suyun, Bao Yayun, Bao Meiyun, etc. There are five Clouds in total. For example, after marrying a Bao Suyun, and then adding one, it is still called Bao Suyun. A guest, two festivals ago, asked for Bao Suyun. Suddenly he went out for half a year. When he returned to Shanghai and went to call for Bao Suyun again, Bao Suyun actually came, but it was already another person. It gives people the feeling that the name is there, but the person is not. They often innovate in this way. They pass it down from generation to generation. Therefore, they often use these names to promote and attract customers. Only the host remains unmoved. They call her the main family. The main family also has daughters. Some still teach them to sell their smiles and carry on their family business. Some say that they will no longer teach them to eat this bowl of food that breaks lives. Either they are sent to a girls' school on Sanma Road to study, or they are taught in a small room, not allowing them to come out to do business. At first, they say it is very good. They also know that opening a house is a sinful thing. It breaks the chastity of many good women and spoils the character of many good children. They think that after they have a little money, they will wash their hands and not do it anymore. But their environment makes them do it. His daughter will still eventually go down this road of prostitution. As the saying goes, "A dragon raises a dragon, a phoenix raises a phoenix, and a thief raises a son who digs holes in the wall." Scholars call it a scholar's family. Those who open a brothel can only be called a family that sells smiles. Therefore, the daughters and daughters-in-law of this kind of main family are often called small main families. Small main families are very good at their job. Because the ladies they take in and buy are always changing, only the small main family guards the main camp. They are in charge of everything there. The A-su that Long Ziyun is talking about is the daughter of the Bao family who opens the house. She is a small main family. She is only nineteen years old this year. She is tall and slender, with charming eyes and a smoky gait. She is the sweetest and most beautiful sister who accompanies the game. First of all, she is good at socializing. She speaks one kind of words to that kind of guest. Moreover, she is humorous and talks and laughs lively. She is truly a smart and clever person. If there is really an exam for a major in social studies in the world, in an era where there is no gender distinction, she would definitely be able to get a doctorate in social studies.

US Cotton Slightly Improved Last Week 201

The New York telegram reported on the cotton market for the week: The low government cotton production estimates for last Saturday caused the short covering to begin, and the market improved. However, due to the poor stock and grain market, the selling trend resumed. Afterwards, the industry bought stocks, which also improved slightly, and the shorts covered their positions again, so the overall trend stabilized. There was not much selling in the South. The cooperative association has a more stable statistical position for standard cotton fabric in January based on the spot goods produced by the (New York) generation, so the cotton factory's outlook is also bright. Generally, it is believed that the lowest peak of the market price has already been seen in the middle of last month, so everyone has the intention to stick to it. However, whether the price can stand firm after the rise depends on the development of transactions. The weekend statistics are attached below (unit: thousands of bales).

Flour Market Continues to Decline 203

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, all months showed a downward trend. The price of foreign wheat in Chicago fell by another four, five, or six cents, and in Canada by another one or twelve cents. As a result, most people's minds were unsettled. With food prices falling so dramatically, it seemed that the whole world was suffering the same pain. Although the situation in China was different, given the overall environment, it was beyond the ability of any one entity to prop up the market. Therefore, although manufacturers' sales were not very smooth, the market finally declined slightly. However, Fufeng Mill, because Australian wheat had been quoted as low as 4.345 taels, although it sold off a significant number of standards, after careful observation, a turnaround was still unlikely. In conclusion, the current month fell by 1 cent compared to the previous day, December, January, and March fell by 1.25 cents, February and April each fell by 1.5 cents, and May fell by 1.5 cents.

Wheat Market Weakens Further 204

Yesterday, after the opening of the futures wheat market in the morning and afternoon, the market generally showed a weakening trend. Although foreign wheat prices continued to fall sharply, the bulls in the current month, with very little high-quality domestic wheat available, still wanted to hold on. The long-term bears were eager to try, but they were held back by the current month, so the decline was limited. However, the environment was still unfavorable. If there is a surplus of actual goods in the future, people's confidence may collapse. As a result, the current month fell by 1 cent compared to the previous day, December fell by 2 cents, January fell by 2 cents, February fell by 3 cents, March fell by 2 cents, and April fell by 1 cent. The spot market was completely stagnant because foreign wheat was gradually being imported by various factories, reducing the need. There were no transactions reported throughout the city.

North-South Goods Black Dates Market Trends Stable 205

Recently, not many black dates have arrived. It is estimated that there are about 5,000 packages in stock on the market. Currently, sales are brisk for mid- and low-grade dates, while high-grade dates are not very active. However, land prices are trending stably. The Shanghai market has also stabilized. Yesterday's market prices were as follows: top-grade date heads, 18 taels; top Gao Zhuang, 13 taels; second Gao Zhuang, 11 taels; Gao Tong Shou, 10 taels; Zhong Tong Shou, 9 taels; and second-grade dates, 7.5 taels.

Silk and Tea, Gongxi Tea Russian Sales Continue Briskly 206

Yesterday, in the local foreign merchant tea market, Russian Aid Society purchases of Gongxi green tea from Lailu Zhuang were still small. The city-wide transaction was over 1,500 boxes. Market prices did not rise or fall compared to the previous day. Judging from the current situation, there is hope that the Russian market will also open for top and middle-grade Zhenmei tea, as tea prices have fallen to the extreme, gradually meeting the needs of that market. In addition, needle-like eyebrow tea and pearl tea were also slightly purchased by British and French merchants. As for black tea, it remained sluggish, and it was feared that the inventory would be difficult to clear.

Hardware, English Steel Plate List Price Plummets 207

The listed price of English steel plates was still relatively stable, but actual transactions were sluggish, so those holding the goods occasionally showed signs of anxiety. In recent days, overseas list prices have plummeted by three or four yuan, causing local standards to also trend downward. In addition, imports are increasing daily, and inventories are becoming more abundant, making it even harder to maintain standards. Currently, 2.5 li is only selling for 9.25 taels, half li for 6.75 taels, 7.5 li for 6.35 taels, 1 fen for 6 taels, and above 1.5 fen, because the arrivals are relatively fresh, can still be maintained at 6.25 taels. Although business in the Yangtze River and Tianjin areas is gradually developing, people's morale is low, and the market atmosphere is weak, resulting in a general sense of fatigue and listlessness in the trend.
