Business News 209

▲ Huiluo Company, located at the corner of Nanjing Road and Sichuan Road, announced that unfortunately, a fire broke out on the fifth and sixth floors of the company a few days ago, and the goods in each department were slightly water-stained. All sectors are welcome to come in and visit. This unexpected loss for the company is a rare opportunity for customers. Be sure to come early to choose and buy to avoid missing out.

New Invention of Zhongling Machine-Printed Photos 210

Hanli Company of this port announced that the company's newly produced Zhongling steam-powered printing press, with its exquisite printing, is praised by all sectors. Recently, the inventor, Mr. Zhongling, used steam pressure to print photos using scientific research. The first experiment was very successful. Purely using optics, the shadow image is first placed on a glass plate, then wiped with a specially made potion, and rolled with ink paste, and an instant photo is created. It is extremely quick and clear, and it is a hundred times better than photos printed by copperplate. No matter what kind of paper or how many copies you want to print, you can print them immediately. The results are on display at the company's distribution office at 161 Wangping Street. All are welcome to visit.

Medical News 211

▲ Dr. Fang Jing'an, a Western medicine practitioner, specializes in obstetrics, gynecology, and pediatrics. Her surgical skills are quick and appropriate, and her diagnoses are accurate. She has served as the director of obstetrics and gynecology at Taizhou Boji Hospital and Wenling County Hospital for many years. This year, at the invitation of relatives and friends in Shanghai, she opened a clinic in Huishan Lane, Ti Lan Bridge. People have been coming to her for treatment in an endless stream. In order to provide assistance to the poor and sick, she has set aside 9:00 AM to 2:00 PM every day as consultation hours, charging only 20 cents for the registration fee. Her fee for delivering babies at home has also been reduced to 10 yuan.

Calligraphy and Painting News 212

▲ Calligrapher and painter Yu Jianhua will hold an exhibition of his recent masterpieces at the Ningbo Fellow Association on the fourth floor. This was reported in a previous newspaper. The opening date was the 15th. Visitors were extremely enthusiastic, and there was a great crowd. All of the exhibited works had already been pre-ordered before the exhibition. Therefore, the second exhibition has been scheduled for December 20th and 21st of the lunar calendar, still at the original location. There are many pre-orders, especially for the two paintings, "Nanshan Cui" (No. 33) and "Qiujiang Wandu" (No. 86), which are very popular. More than ten people have re-ordered each painting, which is a rare sight in the Shanghai calligraphy and painting world. The venue also displays Mr. Yu's articles and Tu Yiru's artistic photography. Viewers linger, praising and admiring, and are reluctant to leave.

Publishing News 213

▲ Wu Hanfang's New Book, "Chinese Human Geography": Professor Wu Hanfang of Daxia University and Chizhi University is one of the few geography experts in the country. He previously authored the book "Philippine Inspection Record," which was published by the Shanghai Commercial Press and was an instant hit. This year, during the first semester, Mr. Wu taught at Fudan University and compiled his usual lectures on Chinese Human Geography, which was published by the Shanghai Beixin Bookstore. The book describes the current situation of China's industry, politics, transportation, education, population, etc. The content is rich, and the materials are new and original. It is an essential book for school textbooks, county magistrate examinations, and those who study the current situation of Chinese society. It is said that it will be published within this month.

▲ Chen Xisheng compiled "Fire Prevention Method." It contains discussions on fire issues and methods to prevent terrible fire disasters. He pays special attention to methods of escaping in times of disaster. The book is written in simple language and is very easy to understand. At this time of dry weather, fires are most likely to occur. Everyone should have common sense in times of disaster. Everyone should have a copy to deal with emergencies. It is now heard that the editor has specially allocated 5,000 copies to be given away to all sectors. Anyone who sends a postal request from within or outside the city and attaches two cents of postage will receive a free copy to show the limit. Contact the Daiyue Company at 329 Jiangxi Road, Shanghai.
